81//#define IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_truetype.h"
82//#define IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME "my_folder/stb_rect_pack.h"

84//#define IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION

86#ifdef IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
87namespace IMGUI_STB_NAMESPACE
88{
89#endif
90
91#ifdef _MSC_VER
92#pragma warning (push)
93#pragma warning (disable: 4456) // declaration of 'xx' hides previous local declaration
94#pragma warning (disable: 6011) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer 'cur->next'.
95#pragma warning (disable: 6385) // (stb_truetype) Reading invalid data from 'buffer': the readable size is '_Old_3`kernel_width' bytes, but '3' bytes may be read.
96#pragma warning (disable: 28182) // (stb_rectpack) Dereferencing NULL pointer. 'cur' contains the same NULL value as 'cur->next' did.
97#endif
98
99#if defined(__clang__)
100#pragma clang diagnostic push
101#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wunused-function"
102#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wmissing-prototypes"
103#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wimplicit-fallthrough"
104#pragma clang diagnostic ignored "-Wcast-qual" // warning: cast from 'const xxxx *' to 'xxx *' drops const qualifier
105#endif
106
107#if defined(__GNUC__)
108#pragma GCC diagnostic push
109#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored "-Wtype-limits" // warning: comparison is always true due to limited range of data type [-Wtype-limits]
110#pragma GCC diagnostic ignored "-Wcast-qual" // warning: cast from type 'const xxxx *' to type 'xxxx *' casts away qualifiers
111#endif

113#ifndef STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit (e.g. unity builds)
114#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another compilation unit
115#define STBRP_STATIC
116#define STBRP_ASSERT(x) do { IM_ASSERT(x); } while (0)
117#define STBRP_SORT ImQsort
118#define STB_RECT_PACK_IMPLEMENTATION
119#endif
120#ifdef IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
121#include IMGUI_STB_RECT_PACK_FILENAME
122#else
123#include "imstb_rectpack.h"
124#endif
125#endif
126
127#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
128#ifndef STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in the _same_ compilation unit (e.g. unity builds)
129#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION // in case the user already have an implementation in another compilation unit
130#define STBTT_malloc(x,u) ((void)(u), IM_ALLOC(x))
131#define STBTT_free(x,u) ((void)(u), IM_FREE(x))
132#define STBTT_assert(x) do { IM_ASSERT(x); } while(0)
133#define STBTT_fmod(x,y) ImFmod(x,y)
134#define STBTT_sqrt(x) ImSqrt(x)
135#define STBTT_pow(x,y) ImPow(x,y)
136#define STBTT_fabs(x) ImFabs(x)
137#define STBTT_ifloor(x) ((int)ImFloorSigned(x))
138#define STBTT_iceil(x) ((int)ImCeil(x))
139#define STBTT_STATIC
140#define STB_TRUETYPE_IMPLEMENTATION
141#else
142#define STBTT_DEF extern
143#endif
144#ifdef IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
145#include IMGUI_STB_TRUETYPE_FILENAME
146#else
147#include "imstb_truetype.h"
148#endif
149#endif
150#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE

174{

293// Those light colors are better suited with a thicker font than the default one + FrameBorder
294void ImGui::StyleColorsLight(ImGuiStyle* dst)
295{
296 ImGuiStyle* style = dst ? dst : &ImGui::GetStyle();

354//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
355// [SECTION] ImDrawList
356//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
357
358ImDrawListSharedData::ImDrawListSharedData()
359{
360 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
361 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx); i++)
362 {
363 const float a = ((float)i * 2 * IM_PI) / (float)IM_ARRAYSIZE(ArcFastVtx);
364 ArcFastVtx[i] = ImVec2(ImCos(a), ImSin(a));
365 }
366 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
367}
368
369void ImDrawListSharedData::SetCircleTessellationMaxError(float max_error)
370{
371 if (CircleSegmentMaxError == max_error)
372 return;
373
374 IM_ASSERT(max_error > 0.0f);
375 CircleSegmentMaxError = max_error;
376 for (int i = 0; i < IM_ARRAYSIZE(CircleSegmentCounts); i++)
377 {
378 const float radius = (float)i;
379 CircleSegmentCounts[i] = (ImU8)((i > 0) ? IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, CircleSegmentMaxError) : IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX);
380 }
381 ArcFastRadiusCutoff = IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC_R(IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, CircleSegmentMaxError);
382}
383
384// Initialize before use in a new frame. We always have a command ready in the buffer.
385void ImDrawList::_ResetForNewFrame()
386{
387 // Verify that the ImDrawCmd fields we want to memcmp() are contiguous in memory.
388 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(IM_OFFSETOF(ImDrawCmd, ClipRect) == 0);
389 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(IM_OFFSETOF(ImDrawCmd, TextureId) == sizeof(ImVec4));
390 IM_STATIC_ASSERT(IM_OFFSETOF(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) == sizeof(ImVec4) + sizeof(ImTextureID));
391 if (_Splitter._Count > 1)
392 _Splitter.Merge(this);
393
394 CmdBuffer.resize(0);
395 IdxBuffer.resize(0);
396 VtxBuffer.resize(0);
397 Flags = _Data->InitialFlags;
398 memset(&_CmdHeader, 0, sizeof(_CmdHeader));
399 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
400 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
401 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
402 _ClipRectStack.resize(0);
403 _TextureIdStack.resize(0);
404 _Path.resize(0);
405 _Splitter.Clear();
406 CmdBuffer.push_back(ImDrawCmd());
407 _FringeScale = 1.0f;
408}
409
410void ImDrawList::_ClearFreeMemory()
411{
412 CmdBuffer.clear();
413 IdxBuffer.clear();
414 VtxBuffer.clear();
415 Flags = ImDrawListFlags_None;
416 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
417 _VtxWritePtr = NULL;
418 _IdxWritePtr = NULL;
419 _ClipRectStack.clear();
420 _TextureIdStack.clear();
421 _Path.clear();
422 _Splitter.ClearFreeMemory();
423}
424
425ImDrawList* ImDrawList::CloneOutput() const
426{
427 ImDrawList* dst = IM_NEW(ImDrawList(_Data));
428 dst->CmdBuffer = CmdBuffer;
429 dst->IdxBuffer = IdxBuffer;
430 dst->VtxBuffer = VtxBuffer;
431 dst->Flags = Flags;
432 return dst;
433}
434
435void ImDrawList::AddDrawCmd()
436{
437 ImDrawCmd draw_cmd;
438 draw_cmd.ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect; // Same as calling ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy()
439 draw_cmd.TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
440 draw_cmd.VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
441 draw_cmd.IdxOffset = IdxBuffer.Size;
442
443 IM_ASSERT(draw_cmd.ClipRect.x <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.z && draw_cmd.ClipRect.y <= draw_cmd.ClipRect.w);
444 CmdBuffer.push_back(draw_cmd);
445}
446
447// Pop trailing draw command (used before merging or presenting to user)
448// Note that this leaves the ImDrawList in a state unfit for further commands, as most code assume that CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL
449void ImDrawList::_PopUnusedDrawCmd()
450{
451 while (CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
452 {
453 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
454 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 || curr_cmd->UserCallback != NULL)
455 return;// break;
456 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
457 }
458}
459
460void ImDrawList::AddCallback(ImDrawCallback callback, void* callback_data)
461{
462 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
463 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
464 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
465 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
466 {
467 AddDrawCmd();
468 curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
469 }
470 curr_cmd->UserCallback = callback;
471 curr_cmd->UserCallbackData = callback_data;
472
473 AddDrawCmd(); // Force a new command after us (see comment below)
474}
475
476// Compare ClipRect, TextureId and VtxOffset with a single memcmp()
477#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize (IM_OFFSETOF(ImDrawCmd, VtxOffset) + sizeof(unsigned int))
478#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS) (memcmp(CMD_LHS, CMD_RHS, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Compare ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
479#define ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC) (memcpy(CMD_DST, CMD_SRC, ImDrawCmd_HeaderSize)) // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
480#define ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(CMD_0, CMD_1) (CMD_0->IdxOffset + CMD_0->ElemCount == CMD_1->IdxOffset)
481
482// Try to merge two last draw commands
483void ImDrawList::_TryMergeDrawCmds()
484{
485 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
486 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
487 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
488 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
489 {
490 prev_cmd->ElemCount += curr_cmd->ElemCount;
491 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
492 }
493}
494
495// Our scheme may appears a bit unusual, basically we want the most-common calls AddLine AddRect etc. to not have to perform any check so we always have a command ready in the stack.
496// The cost of figuring out if a new command has to be added or if we can merge is paid in those Update** functions only.
497void ImDrawList::_OnChangedClipRect()
498{
499 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
500 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
501 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
502 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && memcmp(&curr_cmd->ClipRect, &_CmdHeader.ClipRect, sizeof(ImVec4)) != 0)
503 {
504 AddDrawCmd();
505 return;
506 }
507 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
508
509 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
510 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
511 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
512 {
513 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
514 return;
515 }
516
517 curr_cmd->ClipRect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
518}
519
520void ImDrawList::_OnChangedTextureID()
521{
522 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
523 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
524 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
525 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0 && curr_cmd->TextureId != _CmdHeader.TextureId)
526 {
527 AddDrawCmd();
528 return;
529 }
530 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
531
532 // Try to merge with previous command if it matches, else use current command
533 ImDrawCmd* prev_cmd = curr_cmd - 1;
534 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0 && CmdBuffer.Size > 1 && ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(&_CmdHeader, prev_cmd) == 0 && ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset(prev_cmd, curr_cmd) && prev_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
535 {
536 CmdBuffer.pop_back();
537 return;
538 }
539
540 curr_cmd->TextureId = _CmdHeader.TextureId;
541}
542
543void ImDrawList::_OnChangedVtxOffset()
544{
545 // We don't need to compare curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset because we know it'll be different at the time we call this.
546 _VtxCurrentIdx = 0;
547 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(CmdBuffer.Size > 0);
548 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
549 //IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->VtxOffset != _CmdHeader.VtxOffset); // See #3349
550 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount != 0)
551 {
552 AddDrawCmd();
553 return;
554 }
555 IM_ASSERT(curr_cmd->UserCallback == NULL);
556 curr_cmd->VtxOffset = _CmdHeader.VtxOffset;
557}
558
559int ImDrawList::_CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(float radius) const
560{
561 // Automatic segment count
562 const int radius_idx = (int)(radius + 0.999999f); // ceil to never reduce accuracy
563 if (radius_idx < IM_ARRAYSIZE(_Data->CircleSegmentCounts))
564 return _Data->CircleSegmentCounts[radius_idx]; // Use cached value
565 else
566 return IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_CALC(radius, _Data->CircleSegmentMaxError);
567}
568
569// Render-level scissoring. This is passed down to your render function but not used for CPU-side coarse clipping. Prefer using higher-level ImGui::PushClipRect() to affect logic (hit-testing and widget culling)
570void ImDrawList::PushClipRect(const ImVec2& cr_min, const ImVec2& cr_max, bool intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
571{
572 ImVec4 cr(cr_min.x, cr_min.y, cr_max.x, cr_max.y);
573 if (intersect_with_current_clip_rect)
574 {
575 ImVec4 current = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
576 if (cr.x < current.x) cr.x = current.x;
577 if (cr.y < current.y) cr.y = current.y;
578 if (cr.z > current.z) cr.z = current.z;
579 if (cr.w > current.w) cr.w = current.w;
580 }
581 cr.z = ImMax(cr.x, cr.z);
582 cr.w = ImMax(cr.y, cr.w);
583
584 _ClipRectStack.push_back(cr);
585 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = cr;
586 _OnChangedClipRect();
587}
588
589void ImDrawList::PushClipRectFullScreen()
590{
591 PushClipRect(ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.x, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.y), ImVec2(_Data->ClipRectFullscreen.z, _Data->ClipRectFullscreen.w));
592}
593
594void ImDrawList::PopClipRect()
595{
596 _ClipRectStack.pop_back();
597 _CmdHeader.ClipRect = (_ClipRectStack.Size == 0) ? _Data->ClipRectFullscreen : _ClipRectStack.Data[_ClipRectStack.Size - 1];
598 _OnChangedClipRect();
599}
600
601void ImDrawList::PushTextureID(ImTextureID texture_id)
602{
603 _TextureIdStack.push_back(texture_id);
604 _CmdHeader.TextureId = texture_id;
605 _OnChangedTextureID();
606}
607
608void ImDrawList::PopTextureID()
609{
610 _TextureIdStack.pop_back();
611 _CmdHeader.TextureId = (_TextureIdStack.Size == 0) ? (ImTextureID)NULL : _TextureIdStack.Data[_TextureIdStack.Size - 1];
612 _OnChangedTextureID();
613}
614
615// Reserve space for a number of vertices and indices.
616// You must finish filling your reserved data before calling PrimReserve() again, as it may reallocate or
617// submit the intermediate results. PrimUnreserve() can be used to release unused allocations.
618void ImDrawList::PrimReserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
619{
620 // Large mesh support (when enabled)
621 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
622 if (sizeof(ImDrawIdx) == 2 && (_VtxCurrentIdx + vtx_count >= (1 << 16)) && (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AllowVtxOffset))
623 {
624 // FIXME: In theory we should be testing that vtx_count <64k here.
625 // In practice, RenderText() relies on reserving ahead for a worst case scenario so it is currently useful for us
626 // to not make that check until we rework the text functions to handle clipping and large horizontal lines better.
627 _CmdHeader.VtxOffset = VtxBuffer.Size;
628 _OnChangedVtxOffset();
629 }
630
631 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
632 draw_cmd->ElemCount += idx_count;
633
634 int vtx_buffer_old_size = VtxBuffer.Size;
635 VtxBuffer.resize(vtx_buffer_old_size + vtx_count);
636 _VtxWritePtr = VtxBuffer.Data + vtx_buffer_old_size;
637
638 int idx_buffer_old_size = IdxBuffer.Size;
639 IdxBuffer.resize(idx_buffer_old_size + idx_count);
640 _IdxWritePtr = IdxBuffer.Data + idx_buffer_old_size;
641}
642
643// Release the a number of reserved vertices/indices from the end of the last reservation made with PrimReserve().
644void ImDrawList::PrimUnreserve(int idx_count, int vtx_count)
645{
646 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(idx_count >= 0 && vtx_count >= 0);
647
648 ImDrawCmd* draw_cmd = &CmdBuffer.Data[CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
649 draw_cmd->ElemCount -= idx_count;
650 VtxBuffer.shrink(VtxBuffer.Size - vtx_count);
651 IdxBuffer.shrink(IdxBuffer.Size - idx_count);
652}
653
654// Fully unrolled with inline call to keep our debug builds decently fast.
655void ImDrawList::PrimRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, ImU32 col)
656{
657 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv(_Data->TexUvWhitePixel);
658 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
659 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
660 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
661 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
662 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
663 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
664 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
665 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
666 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
667 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
668}
669
670void ImDrawList::PrimRectUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_c, ImU32 col)
671{
672 ImVec2 b(c.x, a.y), d(a.x, c.y), uv_b(uv_c.x, uv_a.y), uv_d(uv_a.x, uv_c.y);
673 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
674 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
675 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
676 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
677 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
678 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
679 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
680 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
681 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
682 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
683}
684
685void ImDrawList::PrimQuadUV(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& c, const ImVec2& d, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, const ImVec2& uv_c, const ImVec2& uv_d, ImU32 col)
686{
687 ImDrawIdx idx = (ImDrawIdx)_VtxCurrentIdx;
688 _IdxWritePtr[0] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2);
689 _IdxWritePtr[3] = idx; _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx+3);
690 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = a; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv_a; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
691 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = b; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv_b; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
692 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = c; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = uv_c; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
693 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = d; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = uv_d; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
694 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
695 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
696 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
697}
698
699// On AddPolyline() and AddConvexPolyFilled() we intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and superfluous function calls to optimize debug/non-inlined builds.
700// - Those macros expects l-values and need to be used as their own statement.
701// - Those macros are intentionally not surrounded by the 'do {} while (0)' idiom because even that translates to runtime with debug compilers.
702#define IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.0f) { float inv_len = ImRsqrt(d2); VX *= inv_len; VY *= inv_len; } } (void)0
703#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2 100.0f // 500.0f (see #4053, #3366)
704#define IM_FIXNORMAL2F(VX,VY) { float d2 = VX*VX + VY*VY; if (d2 > 0.000001f) { float inv_len2 = 1.0f / d2; if (inv_len2 > IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2) inv_len2 = IM_FIXNORMAL2F_MAX_INVLEN2; VX *= inv_len2; VY *= inv_len2; } } (void)0
705
706// TODO: Thickness anti-aliased lines cap are missing their AA fringe.
707// We avoid using the ImVec2 math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
708void ImDrawList::AddPolyline(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
709{
710 if (points_count < 2 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
711 return;
712
713 const bool closed = (flags & ImDrawFlags_Closed) != 0;
714 const ImVec2 opaque_uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
715 const int count = closed ? points_count : points_count - 1; // The number of line segments we need to draw
716 const bool thick_line = (thickness > _FringeScale);
717
718 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
719 {
720 // Anti-aliased stroke
721 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
722 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
723
724 // Thicknesses <1.0 should behave like thickness 1.0
725 thickness = ImMax(thickness, 1.0f);
726 const int integer_thickness = (int)thickness;
727 const float fractional_thickness = thickness - integer_thickness;
728
729 // Do we want to draw this line using a texture?
730 // - For now, only draw integer-width lines using textures to avoid issues with the way scaling occurs, could be improved.
731 // - If AA_SIZE is not 1.0f we cannot use the texture path.
732 const bool use_texture = (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex) && (integer_thickness < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX) && (fractional_thickness <= 0.00001f) && (AA_SIZE == 1.0f);
733
734 // We should never hit this, because NewFrame() doesn't set ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLinesUseTex unless ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines is off
735 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(!use_texture || !(_Data->Font->ContainerAtlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines));
736
737 const int idx_count = use_texture ? (count * 6) : (thick_line ? count * 18 : count * 12);
738 const int vtx_count = use_texture ? (points_count * 2) : (thick_line ? points_count * 4 : points_count * 3);
739 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
740
741 // Temporary buffer
742 // The first <points_count> items are normals at each line point, then after that there are either 2 or 4 temp points for each line point
743 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count * ((use_texture || !thick_line) ? 3 : 5));
744 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
745 ImVec2* temp_points = temp_normals + points_count;
746
747 // Calculate normals (tangents) for each line segment
748 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
749 {
750 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
751 float dx = points[i2].x - points[i1].x;
752 float dy = points[i2].y - points[i1].y;
753 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
754 temp_normals[i1].x = dy;
755 temp_normals[i1].y = -dx;
756 }
757 if (!closed)
758 temp_normals[points_count - 1] = temp_normals[points_count - 2];
759
760 // If we are drawing a one-pixel-wide line without a texture, or a textured line of any width, we only need 2 or 3 vertices per point
761 if (use_texture || !thick_line)
762 {
763 // [PATH 1] Texture-based lines (thick or non-thick)
764 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (non-thick)
765
766 // The width of the geometry we need to draw - this is essentially <thickness> pixels for the line itself, plus "one pixel" for AA.
767 // - In the texture-based path, we don't use AA_SIZE here because the +1 is tied to the generated texture
768 // (see ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData() function), and so alternate values won't work without changes to that code.
769 // - In the non texture-based paths, we would allow AA_SIZE to potentially be != 1.0f with a patch (e.g. fringe_scale patch to
770 // allow scaling geometry while preserving one-screen-pixel AA fringe).
771 const float half_draw_size = use_texture ? ((thickness * 0.5f) + 1) : AA_SIZE;
772
773 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
774 if (!closed)
775 {
776 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
777 temp_points[1] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * half_draw_size;
778 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+0] = points[points_count-1] + temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
779 temp_points[(points_count-1)*2+1] = points[points_count-1] - temp_normals[points_count-1] * half_draw_size;
780 }
781
782 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
783 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
784 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
785 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
786 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
787 {
788 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1; // i2 is the second point of the line segment
789 const unsigned int idx2 = ((i1 + 1) == points_count) ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + (use_texture ? 2 : 3)); // Vertex index for end of segment
790
791 // Average normals
792 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
793 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
794 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
795 dm_x *= half_draw_size; // dm_x, dm_y are offset to the outer edge of the AA area
796 dm_y *= half_draw_size;
797
798 // Add temporary vertexes for the outer edges
799 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 2];
800 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_x;
801 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_y;
802 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x - dm_x;
803 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y - dm_y;
804
805 if (use_texture)
806 {
807 // Add indices for two triangles
808 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); // Right tri
809 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Left tri
810 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
811 }
812 else
813 {
814 // Add indexes for four triangles
815 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); // Right tri 1
816 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); // Right tri 2
817 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); // Left tri 1
818 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); // Left tri 2
819 _IdxWritePtr += 12;
820 }
821
822 idx1 = idx2;
823 }
824
825 // Add vertexes for each point on the line
826 if (use_texture)
827 {
828 // If we're using textures we only need to emit the left/right edge vertices
829 ImVec4 tex_uvs = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness];
830 /*if (fractional_thickness != 0.0f) // Currently always zero when use_texture==false!
831 {
832 const ImVec4 tex_uvs_1 = _Data->TexUvLines[integer_thickness + 1];
833 tex_uvs.x = tex_uvs.x + (tex_uvs_1.x - tex_uvs.x) * fractional_thickness; // inlined ImLerp()
834 tex_uvs.y = tex_uvs.y + (tex_uvs_1.y - tex_uvs.y) * fractional_thickness;
835 tex_uvs.z = tex_uvs.z + (tex_uvs_1.z - tex_uvs.z) * fractional_thickness;
836 tex_uvs.w = tex_uvs.w + (tex_uvs_1.w - tex_uvs.w) * fractional_thickness;
837 }*/
838 ImVec2 tex_uv0(tex_uvs.x, tex_uvs.y);
839 ImVec2 tex_uv1(tex_uvs.z, tex_uvs.w);
840 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
841 {
842 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = tex_uv0; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Left-side outer edge
843 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = tex_uv1; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col; // Right-side outer edge
844 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
845 }
846 }
847 else
848 {
849 // If we're not using a texture, we need the center vertex as well
850 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
851 {
852 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Center of line
853 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Left-side outer edge
854 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 2 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col_trans; // Right-side outer edge
855 _VtxWritePtr += 3;
856 }
857 }
858 }
859 else
860 {
861 // [PATH 2] Non texture-based lines (thick): we need to draw the solid line core and thus require four vertices per point
862 const float half_inner_thickness = (thickness - AA_SIZE) * 0.5f;
863
864 // If line is not closed, the first and last points need to be generated differently as there are no normals to blend
865 if (!closed)
866 {
867 const int points_last = points_count - 1;
868 temp_points[0] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
869 temp_points[1] = points[0] + temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
870 temp_points[2] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness);
871 temp_points[3] = points[0] - temp_normals[0] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
872 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 0] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
873 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 1] = points[points_last] + temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
874 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 2] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness);
875 temp_points[points_last * 4 + 3] = points[points_last] - temp_normals[points_last] * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
876 }
877
878 // Generate the indices to form a number of triangles for each line segment, and the vertices for the line edges
879 // This takes points n and n+1 and writes into n+1, with the first point in a closed line being generated from the final one (as n+1 wraps)
880 // FIXME-OPT: Merge the different loops, possibly remove the temporary buffer.
881 unsigned int idx1 = _VtxCurrentIdx; // Vertex index for start of line segment
882 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++) // i1 is the first point of the line segment
883 {
884 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : (i1 + 1); // i2 is the second point of the line segment
885 const unsigned int idx2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? _VtxCurrentIdx : (idx1 + 4); // Vertex index for end of segment
886
887 // Average normals
888 float dm_x = (temp_normals[i1].x + temp_normals[i2].x) * 0.5f;
889 float dm_y = (temp_normals[i1].y + temp_normals[i2].y) * 0.5f;
890 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
891 float dm_out_x = dm_x * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
892 float dm_out_y = dm_y * (half_inner_thickness + AA_SIZE);
893 float dm_in_x = dm_x * half_inner_thickness;
894 float dm_in_y = dm_y * half_inner_thickness;
895
896 // Add temporary vertices
897 ImVec2* out_vtx = &temp_points[i2 * 4];
898 out_vtx[0].x = points[i2].x + dm_out_x;
899 out_vtx[0].y = points[i2].y + dm_out_y;
900 out_vtx[1].x = points[i2].x + dm_in_x;
901 out_vtx[1].y = points[i2].y + dm_in_y;
902 out_vtx[2].x = points[i2].x - dm_in_x;
903 out_vtx[2].y = points[i2].y - dm_in_y;
904 out_vtx[3].x = points[i2].x - dm_out_x;
905 out_vtx[3].y = points[i2].y - dm_out_y;
906
907 // Add indexes
908 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2);
909 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
910 _IdxWritePtr[6] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[7] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 1); _IdxWritePtr[8] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0);
911 _IdxWritePtr[9] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[10] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 0); _IdxWritePtr[11] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 1);
912 _IdxWritePtr[12] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[13] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 2); _IdxWritePtr[14] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3);
913 _IdxWritePtr[15] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx1 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[16] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 3); _IdxWritePtr[17] = (ImDrawIdx)(idx2 + 2);
914 _IdxWritePtr += 18;
915
916 idx1 = idx2;
917 }
918
919 // Add vertices
920 for (int i = 0; i < points_count; i++)
921 {
922 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 0]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col_trans;
923 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 1]; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
924 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 2]; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
925 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos = temp_points[i * 4 + 3]; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col_trans;
926 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
927 }
928 }
929 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
930 }
931 else
932 {
933 // [PATH 4] Non texture-based, Non anti-aliased lines
934 const int idx_count = count * 6;
935 const int vtx_count = count * 4; // FIXME-OPT: Not sharing edges
936 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
937
938 for (int i1 = 0; i1 < count; i1++)
939 {
940 const int i2 = (i1 + 1) == points_count ? 0 : i1 + 1;
941 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
942 const ImVec2& p2 = points[i2];
943
944 float dx = p2.x - p1.x;
945 float dy = p2.y - p1.y;
946 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
947 dx *= (thickness * 0.5f);
948 dy *= (thickness * 0.5f);
949
950 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = p1.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = p1.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
951 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = p2.x + dy; _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = p2.y - dx; _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col;
952 _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.x = p2.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[2].pos.y = p2.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[2].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[2].col = col;
953 _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.x = p1.x - dy; _VtxWritePtr[3].pos.y = p1.y + dx; _VtxWritePtr[3].uv = opaque_uv; _VtxWritePtr[3].col = col;
954 _VtxWritePtr += 4;
955
956 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2);
957 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3);
958 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
959 _VtxCurrentIdx += 4;
960 }
961 }
962}
963
964// - We intentionally avoid using ImVec2 and its math operators here to reduce cost to a minimum for debug/non-inlined builds.
965// - Filled shapes must always use clockwise winding order. The anti-aliasing fringe depends on it. Counter-clockwise shapes will have "inward" anti-aliasing.
966void ImDrawList::AddConvexPolyFilled(const ImVec2* points, const int points_count, ImU32 col)
967{
968 if (points_count < 3 || (col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
969 return;
970
971 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
972
973 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedFill)
974 {
975 // Anti-aliased Fill
976 const float AA_SIZE = _FringeScale;
977 const ImU32 col_trans = col & ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
978 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3 + points_count * 6;
979 const int vtx_count = (points_count * 2);
980 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
981
982 // Add indexes for fill
983 unsigned int vtx_inner_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx;
984 unsigned int vtx_outer_idx = _VtxCurrentIdx + 1;
985 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
986 {
987 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + ((i - 1) << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i << 1));
988 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
989 }
990
991 // Compute normals
992 _Data->TempBuffer.reserve_discard(points_count);
993 ImVec2* temp_normals = _Data->TempBuffer.Data;
994 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
995 {
996 const ImVec2& p0 = points[i0];
997 const ImVec2& p1 = points[i1];
998 float dx = p1.x - p0.x;
999 float dy = p1.y - p0.y;
1000 IM_NORMALIZE2F_OVER_ZERO(dx, dy);
1001 temp_normals[i0].x = dy;
1002 temp_normals[i0].y = -dx;
1003 }
1004
1005 for (int i0 = points_count - 1, i1 = 0; i1 < points_count; i0 = i1++)
1006 {
1007 // Average normals
1008 const ImVec2& n0 = temp_normals[i0];
1009 const ImVec2& n1 = temp_normals[i1];
1010 float dm_x = (n0.x + n1.x) * 0.5f;
1011 float dm_y = (n0.y + n1.y) * 0.5f;
1012 IM_FIXNORMAL2F(dm_x, dm_y);
1013 dm_x *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1014 dm_y *= AA_SIZE * 0.5f;
1015
1016 // Add vertices
1017 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.x = (points[i1].x - dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[0].pos.y = (points[i1].y - dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col; // Inner
1018 _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.x = (points[i1].x + dm_x); _VtxWritePtr[1].pos.y = (points[i1].y + dm_y); _VtxWritePtr[1].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[1].col = col_trans; // Outer
1019 _VtxWritePtr += 2;
1020
1021 // Add indexes for fringes
1022 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1));
1023 _IdxWritePtr[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i0 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_outer_idx + (i1 << 1)); _IdxWritePtr[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_inner_idx + (i1 << 1));
1024 _IdxWritePtr += 6;
1025 }
1026 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1027 }
1028 else
1029 {
1030 // Non Anti-aliased Fill
1031 const int idx_count = (points_count - 2)*3;
1032 const int vtx_count = points_count;
1033 PrimReserve(idx_count, vtx_count);
1034 for (int i = 0; i < vtx_count; i++)
1035 {
1036 _VtxWritePtr[0].pos = points[i]; _VtxWritePtr[0].uv = uv; _VtxWritePtr[0].col = col;
1037 _VtxWritePtr++;
1038 }
1039 for (int i = 2; i < points_count; i++)
1040 {
1041 _IdxWritePtr[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx); _IdxWritePtr[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i - 1); _IdxWritePtr[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + i);
1042 _IdxWritePtr += 3;
1043 }
1044 _VtxCurrentIdx += (ImDrawIdx)vtx_count;
1045 }
1046}
1047
1048void ImDrawList::_PathArcToFastEx(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_sample, int a_max_sample, int a_step)
1049{
1050 if (radius < 0.5f)
1051 {
1052 _Path.push_back(center);
1053 return;
1054 }
1055
1056 // Calculate arc auto segment step size
1057 if (a_step <= 0)
1058 a_step = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1059
1060 // Make sure we never do steps larger than one quarter of the circle
1061 a_step = ImClamp(a_step, 1, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_TABLE_SIZE / 4);
1062
1063 const int sample_range = ImAbs(a_max_sample - a_min_sample);
1064 const int a_next_step = a_step;
1065
1066 int samples = sample_range + 1;
1067 bool extra_max_sample = false;
1068 if (a_step > 1)
1069 {
1070 samples = sample_range / a_step + 1;
1071 const int overstep = sample_range % a_step;
1072
1073 if (overstep > 0)
1074 {
1075 extra_max_sample = true;
1076 samples++;
1077
1078 // When we have overstep to avoid awkwardly looking one long line and one tiny one at the end,
1079 // distribute first step range evenly between them by reducing first step size.
1080 if (sample_range > 0)
1081 a_step -= (a_step - overstep) / 2;
1082 }
1083 }
1084
1085 _Path.resize(_Path.Size + samples);
1086 ImVec2* out_ptr = _Path.Data + (_Path.Size - samples);
1087
1088 int sample_index = a_min_sample;
1089 if (sample_index < 0 || sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1090 {
1091 sample_index = sample_index % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1092 if (sample_index < 0)
1093 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1094 }
1095
1096 if (a_max_sample >= a_min_sample)
1097 {
1098 for (int a = a_min_sample; a <= a_max_sample; a += a_step, sample_index += a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1099 {
1100 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1101 if (sample_index >= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX)
1102 sample_index -= IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1103
1104 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1105 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1106 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1107 out_ptr++;
1108 }
1109 }
1110 else
1111 {
1112 for (int a = a_min_sample; a >= a_max_sample; a -= a_step, sample_index -= a_step, a_step = a_next_step)
1113 {
1114 // a_step is clamped to IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, so we have guaranteed that it will not wrap over range twice or more
1115 if (sample_index < 0)
1116 sample_index += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1117
1118 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[sample_index];
1119 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1120 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1121 out_ptr++;
1122 }
1123 }
1124
1125 if (extra_max_sample)
1126 {
1127 int normalized_max_sample = a_max_sample % IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1128 if (normalized_max_sample < 0)
1129 normalized_max_sample += IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1130
1131 const ImVec2 s = _Data->ArcFastVtx[normalized_max_sample];
1132 out_ptr->x = center.x + s.x * radius;
1133 out_ptr->y = center.y + s.y * radius;
1134 out_ptr++;
1135 }
1136
1137 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(_Path.Data + _Path.Size == out_ptr);
1138}
1139
1140void ImDrawList::_PathArcToN(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1141{
1142 if (radius < 0.5f)
1143 {
1144 _Path.push_back(center);
1145 return;
1146 }
1147
1148 // Note that we are adding a point at both a_min and a_max.
1149 // If you are trying to draw a full closed circle you don't want the overlapping points!
1150 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (num_segments + 1));
1151 for (int i = 0; i <= num_segments; i++)
1152 {
1153 const float a = a_min + ((float)i / (float)num_segments) * (a_max - a_min);
1154 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a) * radius));
1155 }
1156}
1157
1158// 0: East, 3: South, 6: West, 9: North, 12: East
1159void ImDrawList::PathArcToFast(const ImVec2& center, float radius, int a_min_of_12, int a_max_of_12)
1160{
1161 if (radius < 0.5f)
1162 {
1163 _Path.push_back(center);
1164 return;
1165 }
1166 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, a_max_of_12 * IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX / 12, 0);
1167}
1168
1169void ImDrawList::PathArcTo(const ImVec2& center, float radius, float a_min, float a_max, int num_segments)
1170{
1171 if (radius < 0.5f)
1172 {
1173 _Path.push_back(center);
1174 return;
1175 }
1176
1177 if (num_segments > 0)
1178 {
1179 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, num_segments);
1180 return;
1181 }
1182
1183 // Automatic segment count
1184 if (radius <= _Data->ArcFastRadiusCutoff)
1185 {
1186 const bool a_is_reverse = a_max < a_min;
1187
1188 // We are going to use precomputed values for mid samples.
1189 // Determine first and last sample in lookup table that belong to the arc.
1190 const float a_min_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_min / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1191 const float a_max_sample_f = IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX * a_max / (IM_PI * 2.0f);
1192
1193 const int a_min_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImFloorSigned(a_min_sample_f) : (int)ImCeil(a_min_sample_f);
1194 const int a_max_sample = a_is_reverse ? (int)ImCeil(a_max_sample_f) : (int)ImFloorSigned(a_max_sample_f);
1195 const int a_mid_samples = a_is_reverse ? ImMax(a_min_sample - a_max_sample, 0) : ImMax(a_max_sample - a_min_sample, 0);
1196
1197 const float a_min_segment_angle = a_min_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1198 const float a_max_segment_angle = a_max_sample * IM_PI * 2.0f / IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX;
1199 const bool a_emit_start = ImAbs(a_min_segment_angle - a_min) >= 1e-5f;
1200 const bool a_emit_end = ImAbs(a_max - a_max_segment_angle) >= 1e-5f;
1201
1202 _Path.reserve(_Path.Size + (a_mid_samples + 1 + (a_emit_start ? 1 : 0) + (a_emit_end ? 1 : 0)));
1203 if (a_emit_start)
1204 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_min) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_min) * radius));
1205 if (a_mid_samples > 0)
1206 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, a_min_sample, a_max_sample, 0);
1207 if (a_emit_end)
1208 _Path.push_back(ImVec2(center.x + ImCos(a_max) * radius, center.y + ImSin(a_max) * radius));
1209 }
1210 else
1211 {
1212 const float arc_length = ImAbs(a_max - a_min);
1213 const int circle_segment_count = _CalcCircleAutoSegmentCount(radius);
1214 const int arc_segment_count = ImMax((int)ImCeil(circle_segment_count * arc_length / (IM_PI * 2.0f)), (int)(2.0f * IM_PI / arc_length));
1215 _PathArcToN(center, radius, a_min, a_max, arc_segment_count);
1216 }
1217}
1218
1219ImVec2 ImBezierCubicCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, float t)
1220{
1221 float u = 1.0f - t;
1222 float w1 = u * u * u;
1223 float w2 = 3 * u * u * t;
1224 float w3 = 3 * u * t * t;
1225 float w4 = t * t * t;
1226 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x + w4 * p4.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y + w4 * p4.y);
1227}
1228
1229ImVec2 ImBezierQuadraticCalc(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, float t)
1230{
1231 float u = 1.0f - t;
1232 float w1 = u * u;
1233 float w2 = 2 * u * t;
1234 float w3 = t * t;
1235 return ImVec2(w1 * p1.x + w2 * p2.x + w3 * p3.x, w1 * p1.y + w2 * p2.y + w3 * p3.y);
1236}
1237
1238// Closely mimics ImBezierCubicClosestPointCasteljau() in imgui.cpp
1239static void PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float x4, float y4, float tess_tol, int level)
1240{
1241 float dx = x4 - x1;
1242 float dy = y4 - y1;
1243 float d2 = (x2 - x4) * dy - (y2 - y4) * dx;
1244 float d3 = (x3 - x4) * dy - (y3 - y4) * dx;
1245 d2 = (d2 >= 0) ? d2 : -d2;
1246 d3 = (d3 >= 0) ? d3 : -d3;
1247 if ((d2 + d3) * (d2 + d3) < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1248 {
1249 path->push_back(ImVec2(x4, y4));
1250 }
1251 else if (level < 10)
1252 {
1253 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1254 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1255 float x34 = (x3 + x4) * 0.5f, y34 = (y3 + y4) * 0.5f;
1256 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1257 float x234 = (x23 + x34) * 0.5f, y234 = (y23 + y34) * 0.5f;
1258 float x1234 = (x123 + x234) * 0.5f, y1234 = (y123 + y234) * 0.5f;
1259 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, x1234, y1234, tess_tol, level + 1);
1260 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(path, x1234, y1234, x234, y234, x34, y34, x4, y4, tess_tol, level + 1);
1261 }
1262}
1263
1264static void PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(ImVector<ImVec2>* path, float x1, float y1, float x2, float y2, float x3, float y3, float tess_tol, int level)
1265{
1266 float dx = x3 - x1, dy = y3 - y1;
1267 float det = (x2 - x3) * dy - (y2 - y3) * dx;
1268 if (det * det * 4.0f < tess_tol * (dx * dx + dy * dy))
1269 {
1270 path->push_back(ImVec2(x3, y3));
1271 }
1272 else if (level < 10)
1273 {
1274 float x12 = (x1 + x2) * 0.5f, y12 = (y1 + y2) * 0.5f;
1275 float x23 = (x2 + x3) * 0.5f, y23 = (y2 + y3) * 0.5f;
1276 float x123 = (x12 + x23) * 0.5f, y123 = (y12 + y23) * 0.5f;
1277 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x1, y1, x12, y12, x123, y123, tess_tol, level + 1);
1278 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(path, x123, y123, x23, y23, x3, y3, tess_tol, level + 1);
1279 }
1280}
1281
1282void ImDrawList::PathBezierCubicCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, int num_segments)
1283{
1284 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1285 if (num_segments == 0)
1286 {
1287 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1288 PathBezierCubicCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, p4.x, p4.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0); // Auto-tessellated
1289 }
1290 else
1291 {
1292 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1293 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1294 _Path.push_back(ImBezierCubicCalc(p1, p2, p3, p4, t_step * i_step));
1295 }
1296}
1297
1298void ImDrawList::PathBezierQuadraticCurveTo(const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, int num_segments)
1299{
1300 ImVec2 p1 = _Path.back();
1301 if (num_segments == 0)
1302 {
1303 IM_ASSERT(_Data->CurveTessellationTol > 0.0f);
1304 PathBezierQuadraticCurveToCasteljau(&_Path, p1.x, p1.y, p2.x, p2.y, p3.x, p3.y, _Data->CurveTessellationTol, 0);// Auto-tessellated
1305 }
1306 else
1307 {
1308 float t_step = 1.0f / (float)num_segments;
1309 for (int i_step = 1; i_step <= num_segments; i_step++)
1310 _Path.push_back(ImBezierQuadraticCalc(p1, p2, p3, t_step * i_step));
1311 }
1312}
1313
1314IM_STATIC_ASSERT(ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft == (1 << 4));
1315static inline ImDrawFlags FixRectCornerFlags(ImDrawFlags flags)
1316{
1317#ifndef IMGUI_DISABLE_OBSOLETE_FUNCTIONS
1318 // Obsoleted in 1.82 (from February 2021)
1319 // Legacy Support for hard coded ~0 (used to be a suggested equivalent to ImDrawCornerFlags_All)
1320 // ~0 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll or 0
1321 if (flags == ~0)
1322 return ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll;
1323
1324 // Legacy Support for hard coded 0x01 to 0x0F (matching 15 out of 16 old flags combinations)
1325 // 0x01 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft (VALUE 0x01 OVERLAPS ImDrawFlags_Closed but ImDrawFlags_Closed is never valid in this path!)
1326 // 0x02 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight
1327 // 0x03 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight
1328 // 0x04 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBotLeft
1329 // 0x05 --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft | ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBotLeft
1330 // ...
1331 // 0x0F --> ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll or 0
1332 // (See all values in ImDrawCornerFlags_)
1333 if (flags >= 0x01 && flags <= 0x0F)
1334 return (flags << 4);
1335
1336 // We cannot support hard coded 0x00 with 'float rounding > 0.0f' --> replace with ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone or use 'float rounding = 0.0f'
1337#endif
1338
1339 // If this triggers, please update your code replacing hardcoded values with new ImDrawFlags_RoundCorners* values.
1340 // Note that ImDrawFlags_Closed (== 0x01) is an invalid flag for AddRect(), AddRectFilled(), PathRect() etc...
1341 IM_ASSERT((flags & 0x0F) == 0 && "Misuse of legacy hardcoded ImDrawCornerFlags values!");
1342
1343 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
1344 flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersAll;
1345
1346 return flags;
1347}
1348
1349void ImDrawList::PathRect(const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1350{
1351 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1352 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.x - a.x) * ( ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTop) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottom) ? 0.5f : 1.0f ) - 1.0f);
1353 rounding = ImMin(rounding, ImFabs(b.y - a.y) * ( ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersLeft) || ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersRight) ? 0.5f : 1.0f ) - 1.0f);
1354
1355 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1356 {
1357 PathLineTo(a);
1358 PathLineTo(ImVec2(b.x, a.y));
1359 PathLineTo(b);
1360 PathLineTo(ImVec2(a.x, b.y));
1361 }
1362 else
1363 {
1364 const float rounding_tl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1365 const float rounding_tr = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1366 const float rounding_br = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1367 const float rounding_bl = (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) ? rounding : 0.0f;
1368 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_tl, a.y + rounding_tl), rounding_tl, 6, 9);
1369 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_tr, a.y + rounding_tr), rounding_tr, 9, 12);
1370 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(b.x - rounding_br, b.y - rounding_br), rounding_br, 0, 3);
1371 PathArcToFast(ImVec2(a.x + rounding_bl, b.y - rounding_bl), rounding_bl, 3, 6);
1372 }
1373}
1374
1375void ImDrawList::AddLine(const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, ImU32 col, float thickness)
1376{
1377 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1378 return;
1379 PathLineTo(p1 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1380 PathLineTo(p2 + ImVec2(0.5f, 0.5f));
1381 PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
1382}
1383
1384// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1385// Note we don't render 1 pixels sized rectangles properly.
1386void ImDrawList::AddRect(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags, float thickness)
1387{
1388 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1389 return;
1390 if (Flags & ImDrawListFlags_AntiAliasedLines)
1391 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), rounding, flags);
1392 else
1393 PathRect(p_min + ImVec2(0.50f, 0.50f), p_max - ImVec2(0.49f, 0.49f), rounding, flags); // Better looking lower-right corner and rounded non-AA shapes.
1394 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1395}
1396
1397void ImDrawList::AddRectFilled(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1398{
1399 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1400 return;
1401 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1402 {
1403 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1404 PrimRect(p_min, p_max, col);
1405 }
1406 else
1407 {
1408 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1409 PathFillConvex(col);
1410 }
1411}
1412
1413// p_min = upper-left, p_max = lower-right
1414void ImDrawList::AddRectFilledMultiColor(const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, ImU32 col_upr_left, ImU32 col_upr_right, ImU32 col_bot_right, ImU32 col_bot_left)
1415{
1416 if (((col_upr_left | col_upr_right | col_bot_right | col_bot_left) & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1417 return;
1418
1419 const ImVec2 uv = _Data->TexUvWhitePixel;
1420 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1421 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 1)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2));
1422 PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 2)); PrimWriteIdx((ImDrawIdx)(_VtxCurrentIdx + 3));
1423 PrimWriteVtx(p_min, uv, col_upr_left);
1424 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_max.x, p_min.y), uv, col_upr_right);
1425 PrimWriteVtx(p_max, uv, col_bot_right);
1426 PrimWriteVtx(ImVec2(p_min.x, p_max.y), uv, col_bot_left);
1427}

1474
1475void ImDrawList::AddCircle(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1476{
1477 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1478 return;
1479
1480 if (num_segments <= 0)
1481 {
1482 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1483 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius - 0.5f, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1484 _Path.Size--;
1485 }
1486 else
1487 {
1488 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1489 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1490
1491 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1492 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1493 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1494 }
1495
1496 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1497}
1498
1499void ImDrawList::AddCircleFilled(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments)
1500{
1501 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || radius < 0.5f)
1502 return;
1503
1504 if (num_segments <= 0)
1505 {
1506 // Use arc with automatic segment count
1507 _PathArcToFastEx(center, radius, 0, IM_DRAWLIST_ARCFAST_SAMPLE_MAX, 0);
1508 _Path.Size--;
1509 }
1510 else
1511 {
1512 // Explicit segment count (still clamp to avoid drawing insanely tessellated shapes)
1513 num_segments = ImClamp(num_segments, 3, IM_DRAWLIST_CIRCLE_AUTO_SEGMENT_MAX);
1514
1515 // Because we are filling a closed shape we remove 1 from the count of segments/points
1516 const float a_max = (IM_PI * 2.0f) * ((float)num_segments - 1.0f) / (float)num_segments;
1517 PathArcTo(center, radius, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1518 }
1519
1520 PathFillConvex(col);
1521}

1523// Guaranteed to honor 'num_segments'
1524void ImDrawList::AddNgon(const ImVec2& center, float radius, ImU32 col, int num_segments, float thickness)
1525{
1526 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0 || num_segments <= 2)
1527 return;

1531 PathArcTo(center, radius - 0.5f, 0.0f, a_max, num_segments - 1);
1532 PathStroke(col, ImDrawFlags_Closed, thickness);
1533}

1545}

1569void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImFont* font, float font_size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, const ImVec4* cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1570{
1571 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1572 return;
1573
1574 if (text_end == NULL)
1575 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin);
1576 if (text_begin == text_end)
1577 return;
1578
1579 // Pull default font/size from the shared ImDrawListSharedData instance
1580 if (font == NULL)
1581 font = _Data->Font;
1582 if (font_size == 0.0f)
1583 font_size = _Data->FontSize;
1584
1585 IM_ASSERT(font->ContainerAtlas->TexID == _CmdHeader.TextureId); // Use high-level ImGui::PushFont() or low-level ImDrawList::PushTextureId() to change font.
1586
1587 ImVec4 clip_rect = _CmdHeader.ClipRect;
1588 if (cpu_fine_clip_rect)
1589 {
1590 clip_rect.x = ImMax(clip_rect.x, cpu_fine_clip_rect->x);
1591 clip_rect.y = ImMax(clip_rect.y, cpu_fine_clip_rect->y);
1592 clip_rect.z = ImMin(clip_rect.z, cpu_fine_clip_rect->z);
1593 clip_rect.w = ImMin(clip_rect.w, cpu_fine_clip_rect->w);
1594 }
1595 font->RenderText(this, font_size, pos, col, clip_rect, text_begin, text_end, wrap_width, cpu_fine_clip_rect != NULL);
1596}
1597
1598void ImDrawList::AddText(const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end)
1599{
1600 AddText(NULL, 0.0f, pos, col, text_begin, text_end);
1601}

1603void ImDrawList::AddImage(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col)
1604{
1605 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1606 return;
1607
1608 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1609 if (push_texture_id)
1610 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1611
1612 PrimReserve(6, 4);
1613 PrimRectUV(p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1614
1615 if (push_texture_id)
1616 PopTextureID();
1617}

1619void ImDrawList::AddImageQuad(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p1, const ImVec2& p2, const ImVec2& p3, const ImVec2& p4, const ImVec2& uv1, const ImVec2& uv2, const ImVec2& uv3, const ImVec2& uv4, ImU32 col)

1622 return;

1625 if (push_texture_id)
1626 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);

1634
1635void ImDrawList::AddImageRounded(ImTextureID user_texture_id, const ImVec2& p_min, const ImVec2& p_max, const ImVec2& uv_min, const ImVec2& uv_max, ImU32 col, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
1636{
1637 if ((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) == 0)
1638 return;
1639
1640 flags = FixRectCornerFlags(flags);
1641 if (rounding < 0.5f || (flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone)
1642 {
1643 AddImage(user_texture_id, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, col);
1644 return;
1645 }
1646
1647 const bool push_texture_id = user_texture_id != _CmdHeader.TextureId;
1648 if (push_texture_id)
1649 PushTextureID(user_texture_id);
1650
1651 int vert_start_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1652 PathRect(p_min, p_max, rounding, flags);
1653 PathFillConvex(col);
1654 int vert_end_idx = VtxBuffer.Size;
1655 ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(this, vert_start_idx, vert_end_idx, p_min, p_max, uv_min, uv_max, true);
1656
1657 if (push_texture_id)
1658 PopTextureID();
1659}
1660
1661
1662//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1663// [SECTION] ImDrawListSplitter
1664//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1665// FIXME: This may be a little confusing, trying to be a little too low-level/optimal instead of just doing vector swap..
1666//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1667
1668void ImDrawListSplitter::ClearFreeMemory()
1669{
1670 for (int i = 0; i < _Channels.Size; i++)
1671 {
1672 if (i == _Current)
1673 memset(&_Channels[i], 0, sizeof(_Channels[i])); // Current channel is a copy of CmdBuffer/IdxBuffer, don't destruct again
1674 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.clear();
1675 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.clear();
1676 }
1677 _Current = 0;
1678 _Count = 1;
1679 _Channels.clear();
1680}
1681
1682void ImDrawListSplitter::Split(ImDrawList* draw_list, int channels_count)
1683{
1684 IM_UNUSED(draw_list);
1685 IM_ASSERT(_Current == 0 && _Count <= 1 && "Nested channel splitting is not supported. Please use separate instances of ImDrawListSplitter.");
1686 int old_channels_count = _Channels.Size;
1687 if (old_channels_count < channels_count)
1688 {
1689 _Channels.reserve(channels_count); // Avoid over reserving since this is likely to stay stable
1690 _Channels.resize(channels_count);
1691 }
1692 _Count = channels_count;
1693
1694 // Channels[] (24/32 bytes each) hold storage that we'll swap with draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
1695 // The content of Channels[0] at this point doesn't matter. We clear it to make state tidy in a debugger but we don't strictly need to.
1696 // When we switch to the next channel, we'll copy draw_list->_CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer into Channels[0] and then Channels[1] into draw_list->CmdBuffer/_IdxBuffer
1697 memset(&_Channels[0], 0, sizeof(ImDrawChannel));
1698 for (int i = 1; i < channels_count; i++)
1699 {
1700 if (i >= old_channels_count)
1701 {
1702 IM_PLACEMENT_NEW(&_Channels[i]) ImDrawChannel();
1703 }
1704 else
1705 {
1706 _Channels[i]._CmdBuffer.resize(0);
1707 _Channels[i]._IdxBuffer.resize(0);
1708 }
1709 }
1710}
1711
1712void ImDrawListSplitter::Merge(ImDrawList* draw_list)
1713{
1714 // Note that we never use or rely on _Channels.Size because it is merely a buffer that we never shrink back to 0 to keep all sub-buffers ready for use.
1715 if (_Count <= 1)
1716 return;
1717
1718 SetCurrentChannel(draw_list, 0);
1719 draw_list->_PopUnusedDrawCmd();
1720
1721 // Calculate our final buffer sizes. Also fix the incorrect IdxOffset values in each command.
1722 int new_cmd_buffer_count = 0;
1723 int new_idx_buffer_count = 0;
1724 ImDrawCmd* last_cmd = (_Count > 0 && draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size > 0) ? &draw_list->CmdBuffer.back() : NULL;
1725 int idx_offset = last_cmd ? last_cmd->IdxOffset + last_cmd->ElemCount : 0;
1726 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
1727 {
1728 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
1729 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().ElemCount == 0 && ch._CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback == NULL) // Equivalent of PopUnusedDrawCmd()
1730 ch._CmdBuffer.pop_back();
1731
1732 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0 && last_cmd != NULL)
1733 {
1734 // Do not include ImDrawCmd_AreSequentialIdxOffset() in the compare as we rebuild IdxOffset values ourselves.
1735 // Manipulating IdxOffset (e.g. by reordering draw commands like done by RenderDimmedBackgroundBehindWindow()) is not supported within a splitter.
1736 ImDrawCmd* next_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer[0];
1737 if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(last_cmd, next_cmd) == 0 && last_cmd->UserCallback == NULL && next_cmd->UserCallback == NULL)
1738 {
1739 // Merge previous channel last draw command with current channel first draw command if matching.
1740 last_cmd->ElemCount += next_cmd->ElemCount;
1741 idx_offset += next_cmd->ElemCount;
1742 ch._CmdBuffer.erase(ch._CmdBuffer.Data); // FIXME-OPT: Improve for multiple merges.
1743 }
1744 }
1745 if (ch._CmdBuffer.Size > 0)
1746 last_cmd = &ch._CmdBuffer.back();
1747 new_cmd_buffer_count += ch._CmdBuffer.Size;
1748 new_idx_buffer_count += ch._IdxBuffer.Size;
1749 for (int cmd_n = 0; cmd_n < ch._CmdBuffer.Size; cmd_n++)
1750 {
1751 ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].IdxOffset = idx_offset;
1752 idx_offset += ch._CmdBuffer.Data[cmd_n].ElemCount;
1753 }
1754 }
1755 draw_list->CmdBuffer.resize(draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size + new_cmd_buffer_count);
1756 draw_list->IdxBuffer.resize(draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + new_idx_buffer_count);
1757
1758 // Write commands and indices in order (they are fairly small structures, we don't copy vertices only indices)
1759 ImDrawCmd* cmd_write = draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data + draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - new_cmd_buffer_count;
1760 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size - new_idx_buffer_count;
1761 for (int i = 1; i < _Count; i++)
1762 {
1763 ImDrawChannel& ch = _Channels[i];
1764 if (int sz = ch._CmdBuffer.Size) { memcpy(cmd_write, ch._CmdBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawCmd)); cmd_write += sz; }
1765 if (int sz = ch._IdxBuffer.Size) { memcpy(idx_write, ch._IdxBuffer.Data, sz * sizeof(ImDrawIdx)); idx_write += sz; }
1766 }
1767 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
1768
1769 // Ensure there's always a non-callback draw command trailing the command-buffer
1770 if (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0 || draw_list->CmdBuffer.back().UserCallback != NULL)
1771 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
1772
1773 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
1774 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
1775 if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
1776 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
1777 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
1778 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
1779
1780 _Count = 1;
1781}
1782
1783void ImDrawListSplitter::SetCurrentChannel(ImDrawList* draw_list, int idx)
1784{
1785 IM_ASSERT(idx >= 0 && idx < _Count);
1786 if (_Current == idx)
1787 return;
1788
1789 // Overwrite ImVector (12/16 bytes), four times. This is merely a silly optimization instead of doing .swap()
1790 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._CmdBuffer, &draw_list->CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
1791 memcpy(&_Channels.Data[_Current]._IdxBuffer, &draw_list->IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
1792 _Current = idx;
1793 memcpy(&draw_list->CmdBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._CmdBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->CmdBuffer));
1794 memcpy(&draw_list->IdxBuffer, &_Channels.Data[idx]._IdxBuffer, sizeof(draw_list->IdxBuffer));
1795 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data + draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size;
1796
1797 // If current command is used with different settings we need to add a new command
1798 ImDrawCmd* curr_cmd = (draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size == 0) ? NULL : &draw_list->CmdBuffer.Data[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1];
1799 if (curr_cmd == NULL)
1800 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
1801 else if (curr_cmd->ElemCount == 0)
1802 ImDrawCmd_HeaderCopy(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader); // Copy ClipRect, TextureId, VtxOffset
1803 else if (ImDrawCmd_HeaderCompare(curr_cmd, &draw_list->_CmdHeader) != 0)
1804 draw_list->AddDrawCmd();
1805}
1806
1807//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1808// [SECTION] ImDrawData
1809//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1810
1811// For backward compatibility: convert all buffers from indexed to de-indexed, in case you cannot render indexed. Note: this is slow and most likely a waste of resources. Always prefer indexed rendering!
1812void ImDrawData::DeIndexAllBuffers()
1813{
1814 ImVector<ImDrawVert> new_vtx_buffer;
1815 TotalVtxCount = TotalIdxCount = 0;
1816 for (int i = 0; i < CmdListsCount; i++)
1817 {
1818 ImDrawList* cmd_list = CmdLists[i];
1819 if (cmd_list->IdxBuffer.empty())
1820 continue;
1821 new_vtx_buffer.resize(cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
1822 for (int j = 0; j < cmd_list->IdxBuffer.Size; j++)
1823 new_vtx_buffer[j] = cmd_list->VtxBuffer[cmd_list->IdxBuffer[j]];
1824 cmd_list->VtxBuffer.swap(new_vtx_buffer);
1825 cmd_list->IdxBuffer.resize(0);
1826 TotalVtxCount += cmd_list->VtxBuffer.Size;
1827 }
1828}
1829
1830// Helper to scale the ClipRect field of each ImDrawCmd.
1831// Use if your final output buffer is at a different scale than draw_data->DisplaySize,
1832// or if there is a difference between your window resolution and framebuffer resolution.
1833void ImDrawData::ScaleClipRects(const ImVec2& fb_scale)
1834{
1835 for (int i = 0; i < CmdListsCount; i++)
1836 {
1837 ImDrawList* cmd_list = CmdLists[i];
1838 for (int cmd_i = 0; cmd_i < cmd_list->CmdBuffer.Size; cmd_i++)
1839 {
1840 ImDrawCmd* cmd = &cmd_list->CmdBuffer[cmd_i];
1841 cmd->ClipRect = ImVec4(cmd->ClipRect.x * fb_scale.x, cmd->ClipRect.y * fb_scale.y, cmd->ClipRect.z * fb_scale.x, cmd->ClipRect.w * fb_scale.y);
1842 }
1843 }
1844}
1845
1846//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1847// [SECTION] Helpers ShadeVertsXXX functions
1848//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
1849
1850// Generic linear color gradient, write to RGB fields, leave A untouched.
1851void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearColorGradientKeepAlpha(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, ImVec2 gradient_p0, ImVec2 gradient_p1, ImU32 col0, ImU32 col1)
1852{
1853 ImVec2 gradient_extent = gradient_p1 - gradient_p0;
1854 float gradient_inv_length2 = 1.0f / ImLengthSqr(gradient_extent);
1855 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
1856 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
1857 const int col0_r = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
1858 const int col0_g = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
1859 const int col0_b = (int)(col0 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF;
1860 const int col_delta_r = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_r;
1861 const int col_delta_g = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_g;
1862 const int col_delta_b = ((int)(col1 >> IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) & 0xFF) - col0_b;
1863 for (ImDrawVert* vert = vert_start; vert < vert_end; vert++)
1864 {
1865 float d = ImDot(vert->pos - gradient_p0, gradient_extent);
1866 float t = ImClamp(d * gradient_inv_length2, 0.0f, 1.0f);
1867 int r = (int)(col0_r + col_delta_r * t);
1868 int g = (int)(col0_g + col_delta_g * t);
1869 int b = (int)(col0_b + col_delta_b * t);
1870 vert->col = (r << IM_COL32_R_SHIFT) | (g << IM_COL32_G_SHIFT) | (b << IM_COL32_B_SHIFT) | (vert->col & IM_COL32_A_MASK);
1871 }
1872}
1873
1874// Distribute UV over (a, b) rectangle
1875void ImGui::ShadeVertsLinearUV(ImDrawList* draw_list, int vert_start_idx, int vert_end_idx, const ImVec2& a, const ImVec2& b, const ImVec2& uv_a, const ImVec2& uv_b, bool clamp)
1876{
1877 const ImVec2 size = b - a;
1878 const ImVec2 uv_size = uv_b - uv_a;
1879 const ImVec2 scale = ImVec2(
1880 size.x != 0.0f ? (uv_size.x / size.x) : 0.0f,
1881 size.y != 0.0f ? (uv_size.y / size.y) : 0.0f);
1882
1883 ImDrawVert* vert_start = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_start_idx;
1884 ImDrawVert* vert_end = draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data + vert_end_idx;
1885 if (clamp)
1886 {
1887 const ImVec2 min = ImMin(uv_a, uv_b);
1888 const ImVec2 max = ImMax(uv_a, uv_b);
1889 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
1890 vertex->uv = ImClamp(uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale), min, max);
1891 }
1892 else
1893 {
1894 for (ImDrawVert* vertex = vert_start; vertex < vert_end; ++vertex)
1895 vertex->uv = uv_a + ImMul(ImVec2(vertex->pos.x, vertex->pos.y) - a, scale);
1896 }
1897}

1907 OversampleH = 3; // FIXME: 2 may be a better default?
1908 OversampleV = 1;
1909 GlyphMaxAdvanceX = FLT_MAX;
1910 RasterizerMultiply = 1.0f;
1911 EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)-1;
1912}

1968ImFontAtlas::ImFontAtlas()
1969{
1970 memset(this, 0, sizeof(*this));
1971 TexGlyphPadding = 1;
1972 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
1973}
1974
1975ImFontAtlas::~ImFontAtlas()
1976{
1977 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
1978 Clear();
1979}
1980
1981void ImFontAtlas::ClearInputData()
1982{
1983 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
1984 for (int i = 0; i < ConfigData.Size; i++)
1985 if (ConfigData[i].FontData && ConfigData[i].FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
1986 {
1987 IM_FREE(ConfigData[i].FontData);
1988 ConfigData[i].FontData = NULL;
1989 }
1990
1991 // When clearing this we lose access to the font name and other information used to build the font.
1992 for (int i = 0; i < Fonts.Size; i++)
1993 if (Fonts[i]->ConfigData >= ConfigData.Data && Fonts[i]->ConfigData < ConfigData.Data + ConfigData.Size)
1994 {
1995 Fonts[i]->ConfigData = NULL;
1996 Fonts[i]->ConfigDataCount = 0;
1997 }
1998 ConfigData.clear();
1999 CustomRects.clear();
2000 PackIdMouseCursors = PackIdLines = -1;
2001 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2002}
2003
2004void ImFontAtlas::ClearTexData()
2005{
2006 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2007 if (TexPixelsAlpha8)
2008 IM_FREE(TexPixelsAlpha8);
2009 if (TexPixelsRGBA32)
2010 IM_FREE(TexPixelsRGBA32);
2011 TexPixelsAlpha8 = NULL;
2012 TexPixelsRGBA32 = NULL;
2013 TexPixelsUseColors = false;
2014 // Important: we leave TexReady untouched
2015}
2016
2017void ImFontAtlas::ClearFonts()
2018{
2019 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2020 Fonts.clear_delete();
2021 TexReady = false;
2022}
2023
2024void ImFontAtlas::Clear()
2025{
2026 ClearInputData();
2027 ClearTexData();
2028 ClearFonts();
2029}
2030
2031void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsAlpha8(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2032{
2033 // Build atlas on demand
2034 if (TexPixelsAlpha8 == NULL)
2035 Build();
2036
2037 *out_pixels = TexPixelsAlpha8;
2038 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2039 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2040 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 1;
2041}
2042
2043void ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAsRGBA32(unsigned char** out_pixels, int* out_width, int* out_height, int* out_bytes_per_pixel)
2044{
2045 // Convert to RGBA32 format on demand
2046 // Although it is likely to be the most commonly used format, our font rendering is 1 channel / 8 bpp
2047 if (!TexPixelsRGBA32)
2048 {
2049 unsigned char* pixels = NULL;
2050 GetTexDataAsAlpha8(&pixels, NULL, NULL);
2051 if (pixels)
2052 {
2053 TexPixelsRGBA32 = (unsigned int*)IM_ALLOC((size_t)TexWidth * (size_t)TexHeight * 4);
2054 const unsigned char* src = pixels;
2055 unsigned int* dst = TexPixelsRGBA32;
2056 for (int n = TexWidth * TexHeight; n > 0; n--)
2057 *dst++ = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, (unsigned int)(*src++));
2058 }
2059 }
2060
2061 *out_pixels = (unsigned char*)TexPixelsRGBA32;
2062 if (out_width) *out_width = TexWidth;
2063 if (out_height) *out_height = TexHeight;
2064 if (out_bytes_per_pixel) *out_bytes_per_pixel = 4;
2065}
2066
2067ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFont(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg)
2068{
2069 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2070 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->FontData != NULL && font_cfg->FontDataSize > 0);
2071 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg->SizePixels > 0.0f);
2072
2073 // Create new font
2074 if (!font_cfg->MergeMode)
2075 Fonts.push_back(IM_NEW(ImFont));
2076 else
2077 IM_ASSERT(!Fonts.empty() && "Cannot use MergeMode for the first font"); // When using MergeMode make sure that a font has already been added before. You can use ImGui::GetIO().Fonts->AddFontDefault() to add the default imgui font.
2078
2079 ConfigData.push_back(*font_cfg);
2080 ImFontConfig& new_font_cfg = ConfigData.back();
2081 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont == NULL)
2082 new_font_cfg.DstFont = Fonts.back();
2083 if (!new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas)
2084 {
2085 new_font_cfg.FontData = IM_ALLOC(new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2086 new_font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2087 memcpy(new_font_cfg.FontData, font_cfg->FontData, (size_t)new_font_cfg.FontDataSize);
2088 }
2089
2090 if (new_font_cfg.DstFont->EllipsisChar == (ImWchar)-1)
2091 new_font_cfg.DstFont->EllipsisChar = font_cfg->EllipsisChar;
2092
2093 // Invalidate texture
2094 TexReady = false;
2095 ClearTexData();
2096 return new_font_cfg.DstFont;
2097}
2098
2099// Default font TTF is compressed with stb_compress then base85 encoded (see misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp for encoder)
2100static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char* input);
2101static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char* output, const unsigned char* input, unsigned int length);
2102static const char* GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTFBase85();
2103static unsigned int Decode85Byte(char c) { return c >= '\\' ? c-36 : c-35; }
2104static void Decode85(const unsigned char* src, unsigned char* dst)
2105{
2106 while (*src)
2107 {
2108 unsigned int tmp = Decode85Byte(src[0]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[1]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[2]) + 85 * (Decode85Byte(src[3]) + 85 * Decode85Byte(src[4]))));
2109 dst[0] = ((tmp >> 0) & 0xFF); dst[1] = ((tmp >> 8) & 0xFF); dst[2] = ((tmp >> 16) & 0xFF); dst[3] = ((tmp >> 24) & 0xFF); // We can't assume little-endianness.
2110 src += 5;
2111 dst += 4;
2112 }
2113}
2114
2115// Load embedded ProggyClean.ttf at size 13, disable oversampling
2116ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontDefault(const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template)
2117{
2118 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2119 if (!font_cfg_template)
2120 {
2121 font_cfg.OversampleH = font_cfg.OversampleV = 1;
2122 font_cfg.PixelSnapH = true;
2123 }
2124 if (font_cfg.SizePixels <= 0.0f)
2125 font_cfg.SizePixels = 13.0f * 1.0f;
2126 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2127 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "ProggyClean.ttf, %dpx", (int)font_cfg.SizePixels);
2128 font_cfg.EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)0x0085;
2129 font_cfg.GlyphOffset.y = 1.0f * IM_FLOOR(font_cfg.SizePixels / 13.0f); // Add +1 offset per 13 units
2130
2131 const char* ttf_compressed_base85 = GetDefaultCompressedFontDataTTFBase85();
2132 const ImWchar* glyph_ranges = font_cfg.GlyphRanges != NULL ? font_cfg.GlyphRanges : GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2133 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(ttf_compressed_base85, font_cfg.SizePixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2134 return font;
2135}
2136
2137ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromFileTTF(const char* filename, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2138{
2139 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2140 size_t data_size = 0;
2141 void* data = ImFileLoadToMemory(filename, "rb", &data_size, 0);
2142 if (!data)
2143 {
2144 IM_ASSERT_USER_ERROR(0, "Could not load font file!");
2145 return NULL;
2146 }
2147 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2148 if (font_cfg.Name[0] == '\0')
2149 {
2150 // Store a short copy of filename into into the font name for convenience
2151 const char* p;
2152 for (p = filename + strlen(filename); p > filename && p[-1] != '/' && p[-1] != '\\'; p--) {}
2153 ImFormatString(font_cfg.Name, IM_ARRAYSIZE(font_cfg.Name), "%s, %.0fpx", p, size_pixels);
2154 }
2155 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(data, (int)data_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2156}
2157
2158// NB: Transfer ownership of 'ttf_data' to ImFontAtlas, unless font_cfg_template->FontDataOwnedByAtlas == false. Owned TTF buffer will be deleted after Build().
2159ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryTTF(void* ttf_data, int ttf_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2160{
2161 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2162 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2163 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2164 font_cfg.FontData = ttf_data;
2165 font_cfg.FontDataSize = ttf_size;
2166 font_cfg.SizePixels = size_pixels > 0.0f ? size_pixels : font_cfg.SizePixels;
2167 if (glyph_ranges)
2168 font_cfg.GlyphRanges = glyph_ranges;
2169 return AddFont(&font_cfg);
2170}
2171
2172ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(const void* compressed_ttf_data, int compressed_ttf_size, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg_template, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2173{
2174 const unsigned int buf_decompressed_size = stb_decompress_length((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data);
2175 unsigned char* buf_decompressed_data = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(buf_decompressed_size);
2176 stb_decompress(buf_decompressed_data, (const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data, (unsigned int)compressed_ttf_size);
2177
2178 ImFontConfig font_cfg = font_cfg_template ? *font_cfg_template : ImFontConfig();
2179 IM_ASSERT(font_cfg.FontData == NULL);
2180 font_cfg.FontDataOwnedByAtlas = true;
2181 return AddFontFromMemoryTTF(buf_decompressed_data, (int)buf_decompressed_size, size_pixels, &font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2182}
2183
2184ImFont* ImFontAtlas::AddFontFromMemoryCompressedBase85TTF(const char* compressed_ttf_data_base85, float size_pixels, const ImFontConfig* font_cfg, const ImWchar* glyph_ranges)
2185{
2186 int compressed_ttf_size = (((int)strlen(compressed_ttf_data_base85) + 4) / 5) * 4;
2187 void* compressed_ttf = IM_ALLOC((size_t)compressed_ttf_size);
2188 Decode85((const unsigned char*)compressed_ttf_data_base85, (unsigned char*)compressed_ttf);
2189 ImFont* font = AddFontFromMemoryCompressedTTF(compressed_ttf, compressed_ttf_size, size_pixels, font_cfg, glyph_ranges);
2190 IM_FREE(compressed_ttf);
2191 return font;
2192}

2194int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectRegular(int width, int height)
2195{
2196 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2197 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2198 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2199 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2200 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2201 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2202 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2203}
