2205int ImFontAtlas::AddCustomRectFontGlyph(ImFont* font, ImWchar id, int width, int height, float advance_x, const ImVec2& offset)
2206{
2207#ifdef IMGUI_USE_WCHAR32
2208 IM_ASSERT(id <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX);
2209#endif
2210 IM_ASSERT(font != NULL);
2211 IM_ASSERT(width > 0 && width <= 0xFFFF);
2212 IM_ASSERT(height > 0 && height <= 0xFFFF);
2213 ImFontAtlasCustomRect r;
2214 r.Width = (unsigned short)width;
2215 r.Height = (unsigned short)height;
2216 r.GlyphID = id;
2217 r.GlyphAdvanceX = advance_x;
2218 r.GlyphOffset = offset;
2219 r.Font = font;
2220 CustomRects.push_back(r);
2221 return CustomRects.Size - 1; // Return index
2222}
2223
2224void ImFontAtlas::CalcCustomRectUV(const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* rect, ImVec2* out_uv_min, ImVec2* out_uv_max) const
2225{
2226 IM_ASSERT(TexWidth > 0 && TexHeight > 0); // Font atlas needs to be built before we can calculate UV coordinates
2227 IM_ASSERT(rect->IsPacked()); // Make sure the rectangle has been packed
2228 *out_uv_min = ImVec2((float)rect->X * TexUvScale.x, (float)rect->Y * TexUvScale.y);
2229 *out_uv_max = ImVec2((float)(rect->X + rect->Width) * TexUvScale.x, (float)(rect->Y + rect->Height) * TexUvScale.y);
2230}
2231
2232bool ImFontAtlas::GetMouseCursorTexData(ImGuiMouseCursor cursor_type, ImVec2* out_offset, ImVec2* out_size, ImVec2 out_uv_border[2], ImVec2 out_uv_fill[2])
2233{
2234 if (cursor_type <= ImGuiMouseCursor_None || cursor_type >= ImGuiMouseCursor_COUNT)
2235 return false;
2236 if (Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors)
2237 return false;
2238
2239 IM_ASSERT(PackIdMouseCursors != -1);
2240 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = GetCustomRectByIndex(PackIdMouseCursors);
2241 ImVec2 pos = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][0] + ImVec2((float)r->X, (float)r->Y);
2242 ImVec2 size = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][1];
2243 *out_size = size;
2244 *out_offset = FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_CURSOR_DATA[cursor_type][2];
2245 out_uv_border[0] = (pos) * TexUvScale;
2246 out_uv_border[1] = (pos + size) * TexUvScale;
2247 pos.x += FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
2248 out_uv_fill[0] = (pos) * TexUvScale;
2249 out_uv_fill[1] = (pos + size) * TexUvScale;
2250 return true;
2251}
2252
2253bool ImFontAtlas::Build()
2254{
2255 IM_ASSERT(!Locked && "Cannot modify a locked ImFontAtlas between NewFrame() and EndFrame/Render()!");
2256
2257 // Default font is none are specified
2258 if (ConfigData.Size == 0)
2259 AddFontDefault();
2260
2261 // Select builder
2262 // - Note that we do not reassign to atlas->FontBuilderIO, since it is likely to point to static data which
2263 // may mess with some hot-reloading schemes. If you need to assign to this (for dynamic selection) AND are
2264 // using a hot-reloading scheme that messes up static data, store your own instance of ImFontBuilderIO somewhere
2265 // and point to it instead of pointing directly to return value of the GetBuilderXXX functions.
2266 const ImFontBuilderIO* builder_io = FontBuilderIO;
2267 if (builder_io == NULL)
2268 {
2269#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_FREETYPE
2270 builder_io = ImGuiFreeType::GetBuilderForFreeType();
2271#elif defined(IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE)
2272 builder_io = ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype();
2273#else
2274 IM_ASSERT(0); // Invalid Build function
2275#endif
2276 }
2277
2278 // Build
2279 return builder_io->FontBuilder_Build(this);
2280}
2281
2282void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(unsigned char out_table[256], float in_brighten_factor)
2283{
2284 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < 256; i++)
2285 {
2286 unsigned int value = (unsigned int)(i * in_brighten_factor);
2287 out_table[i] = value > 255 ? 255 : (value & 0xFF);
2288 }
2289}
2290
2291void ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(const unsigned char table[256], unsigned char* pixels, int x, int y, int w, int h, int stride)
2292{
2293 IM_ASSERT_PARANOID(w <= stride);
2294 unsigned char* data = pixels + x + y * stride;
2295 for (int j = h; j > 0; j--, data += stride - w)
2296 for (int i = w; i > 0; i--, data++)
2297 *data = table[*data];
2298}
2299
2300#ifdef IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
2301// Temporary data for one source font (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2302// (C++03 doesn't allow instancing ImVector<> with function-local types so we declare the type here.)
2303struct ImFontBuildSrcData
2304{
2305 stbtt_fontinfo FontInfo;
2306 stbtt_pack_range PackRange; // Hold the list of codepoints to pack (essentially points to Codepoints.Data)
2307 stbrp_rect* Rects; // Rectangle to pack. We first fill in their size and the packer will give us their position.
2308 stbtt_packedchar* PackedChars; // Output glyphs
2309 const ImWchar* SrcRanges; // Ranges as requested by user (user is allowed to request too much, e.g. 0x0020..0xFFFF)
2310 int DstIndex; // Index into atlas->Fonts[] and dst_tmp_array[]
2311 int GlyphsHighest; // Highest requested codepoint
2312 int GlyphsCount; // Glyph count (excluding missing glyphs and glyphs already set by an earlier source font)
2313 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // Glyph bit map (random access, 1-bit per codepoint. This will be a maximum of 8KB)
2314 ImVector<int> GlyphsList; // Glyph codepoints list (flattened version of GlyphsSet)
2315};
2316
2317// Temporary data for one destination ImFont* (multiple source fonts can be merged into one destination ImFont)
2318struct ImFontBuildDstData
2319{
2320 int SrcCount; // Number of source fonts targeting this destination font.
2321 int GlyphsHighest;
2322 int GlyphsCount;
2323 ImBitVector GlyphsSet; // This is used to resolve collision when multiple sources are merged into a same destination font.
2324};
2325
2326static void UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(const ImBitVector* in, ImVector<int>* out)
2327{
2328 IM_ASSERT(sizeof(in->Storage.Data[0]) == sizeof(int));
2329 const ImU32* it_begin = in->Storage.begin();
2330 const ImU32* it_end = in->Storage.end();
2331 for (const ImU32* it = it_begin; it < it_end; it++)
2332 if (ImU32 entries_32 = *it)
2333 for (ImU32 bit_n = 0; bit_n < 32; bit_n++)
2334 if (entries_32 & ((ImU32)1 << bit_n))
2335 out->push_back((int)(((it - it_begin) << 5) + bit_n));
2336}
2337
2338static bool ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2339{
2340 IM_ASSERT(atlas->ConfigData.Size > 0);
2341
2342 ImFontAtlasBuildInit(atlas);
2343
2344 // Clear atlas
2345 atlas->TexID = (ImTextureID)NULL;
2346 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexHeight = 0;
2347 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2348 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2(0.0f, 0.0f);
2349 atlas->ClearTexData();
2350
2351 // Temporary storage for building
2352 ImVector<ImFontBuildSrcData> src_tmp_array;
2353 ImVector<ImFontBuildDstData> dst_tmp_array;
2354 src_tmp_array.resize(atlas->ConfigData.Size);
2355 dst_tmp_array.resize(atlas->Fonts.Size);
2356 memset(src_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)src_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2357 memset(dst_tmp_array.Data, 0, (size_t)dst_tmp_array.size_in_bytes());
2358
2359 // 1. Initialize font loading structure, check font data validity
2360 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < atlas->ConfigData.Size; src_i++)
2361 {
2362 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2363 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2364 IM_ASSERT(cfg.DstFont && (!cfg.DstFont->IsLoaded() || cfg.DstFont->ContainerAtlas == atlas));
2365
2366 // Find index from cfg.DstFont (we allow the user to set cfg.DstFont. Also it makes casual debugging nicer than when storing indices)
2367 src_tmp.DstIndex = -1;
2368 for (int output_i = 0; output_i < atlas->Fonts.Size && src_tmp.DstIndex == -1; output_i++)
2369 if (cfg.DstFont == atlas->Fonts[output_i])
2370 src_tmp.DstIndex = output_i;
2371 if (src_tmp.DstIndex == -1)
2372 {
2373 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.DstIndex != -1); // cfg.DstFont not pointing within atlas->Fonts[] array?
2374 return false;
2375 }
2376 // Initialize helper structure for font loading and verify that the TTF/OTF data is correct
2377 const int font_offset = stbtt_GetFontOffsetForIndex((unsigned char*)cfg.FontData, cfg.FontNo);
2378 IM_ASSERT(font_offset >= 0 && "FontData is incorrect, or FontNo cannot be found.");
2379 if (!stbtt_InitFont(&src_tmp.FontInfo, (unsigned char*)cfg.FontData, font_offset))
2380 return false;
2381
2382 // Measure highest codepoints
2383 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2384 src_tmp.SrcRanges = cfg.GlyphRanges ? cfg.GlyphRanges : atlas->GetGlyphRangesDefault();
2385 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2386 {
2387 // Check for valid range. This may also help detect *some* dangling pointers, because a common
2388 // user error is to setup ImFontConfig::GlyphRanges with a pointer to data that isn't persistent.
2389 IM_ASSERT(src_range[0] <= src_range[1]);
2390 src_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest, (int)src_range[1]);
2391 }
2392 dst_tmp.SrcCount++;
2393 dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest = ImMax(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest, src_tmp.GlyphsHighest);
2394 }
2395
2396 // 2. For every requested codepoint, check for their presence in the font data, and handle redundancy or overlaps between source fonts to avoid unused glyphs.
2397 int total_glyphs_count = 0;
2398 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2399 {
2400 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2401 ImFontBuildDstData& dst_tmp = dst_tmp_array[src_tmp.DstIndex];
2402 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(src_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2403 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Storage.empty())
2404 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.Create(dst_tmp.GlyphsHighest + 1);
2405
2406 for (const ImWchar* src_range = src_tmp.SrcRanges; src_range[0] && src_range[1]; src_range += 2)
2407 for (unsigned int codepoint = src_range[0]; codepoint <= src_range[1]; codepoint++)
2408 {
2409 if (dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.TestBit(codepoint)) // Don't overwrite existing glyphs. We could make this an option for MergeMode (e.g. MergeOverwrite==true)
2410 continue;
2411 if (!stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, codepoint)) // It is actually in the font?
2412 continue;
2413
2414 // Add to avail set/counters
2415 src_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2416 dst_tmp.GlyphsCount++;
2417 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2418 dst_tmp.GlyphsSet.SetBit(codepoint);
2419 total_glyphs_count++;
2420 }
2421 }
2422
2423 // 3. Unpack our bit map into a flat list (we now have all the Unicode points that we know are requested _and_ available _and_ not overlapping another)
2424 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2425 {
2426 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2427 src_tmp.GlyphsList.reserve(src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2428 UnpackBitVectorToFlatIndexList(&src_tmp.GlyphsSet, &src_tmp.GlyphsList);
2429 src_tmp.GlyphsSet.Clear();
2430 IM_ASSERT(src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size == src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2431 }
2432 for (int dst_i = 0; dst_i < dst_tmp_array.Size; dst_i++)
2433 dst_tmp_array[dst_i].GlyphsSet.Clear();
2434 dst_tmp_array.clear();
2435
2436 // Allocate packing character data and flag packed characters buffer as non-packed (x0=y0=x1=y1=0)
2437 // (We technically don't need to zero-clear buf_rects, but let's do it for the sake of sanity)
2438 ImVector<stbrp_rect> buf_rects;
2439 ImVector<stbtt_packedchar> buf_packedchars;
2440 buf_rects.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2441 buf_packedchars.resize(total_glyphs_count);
2442 memset(buf_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_rects.size_in_bytes());
2443 memset(buf_packedchars.Data, 0, (size_t)buf_packedchars.size_in_bytes());
2444
2445 // 4. Gather glyphs sizes so we can pack them in our virtual canvas.
2446 int total_surface = 0;
2447 int buf_rects_out_n = 0;
2448 int buf_packedchars_out_n = 0;
2449 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2450 {
2451 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2452 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2453 continue;
2454
2455 src_tmp.Rects = &buf_rects[buf_rects_out_n];
2456 src_tmp.PackedChars = &buf_packedchars[buf_packedchars_out_n];
2457 buf_rects_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
2458 buf_packedchars_out_n += src_tmp.GlyphsCount;
2459
2460 // Convert our ranges in the format stb_truetype wants
2461 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2462 src_tmp.PackRange.font_size = cfg.SizePixels;
2463 src_tmp.PackRange.first_unicode_codepoint_in_range = 0;
2464 src_tmp.PackRange.array_of_unicode_codepoints = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Data;
2465 src_tmp.PackRange.num_chars = src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size;
2466 src_tmp.PackRange.chardata_for_range = src_tmp.PackedChars;
2467 src_tmp.PackRange.h_oversample = (unsigned char)cfg.OversampleH;
2468 src_tmp.PackRange.v_oversample = (unsigned char)cfg.OversampleV;
2469
2470 // Gather the sizes of all rectangles we will need to pack (this loop is based on stbtt_PackFontRangesGatherRects)
2471 const float scale = (cfg.SizePixels > 0) ? stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, cfg.SizePixels) : stbtt_ScaleForMappingEmToPixels(&src_tmp.FontInfo, -cfg.SizePixels);
2472 const int padding = atlas->TexGlyphPadding;
2473 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsList.Size; glyph_i++)
2474 {
2475 int x0, y0, x1, y1;
2476 const int glyph_index_in_font = stbtt_FindGlyphIndex(&src_tmp.FontInfo, src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i]);
2477 IM_ASSERT(glyph_index_in_font != 0);
2478 stbtt_GetGlyphBitmapBoxSubpixel(&src_tmp.FontInfo, glyph_index_in_font, scale * cfg.OversampleH, scale * cfg.OversampleV, 0, 0, &x0, &y0, &x1, &y1);
2479 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w = (stbrp_coord)(x1 - x0 + padding + cfg.OversampleH - 1);
2480 src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h = (stbrp_coord)(y1 - y0 + padding + cfg.OversampleV - 1);
2481 total_surface += src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].w * src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h;
2482 }
2483 }
2484
2485 // We need a width for the skyline algorithm, any width!
2486 // The exact width doesn't really matter much, but some API/GPU have texture size limitations and increasing width can decrease height.
2487 // User can override TexDesiredWidth and TexGlyphPadding if they wish, otherwise we use a simple heuristic to select the width based on expected surface.
2488 const int surface_sqrt = (int)ImSqrt((float)total_surface) + 1;
2489 atlas->TexHeight = 0;
2490 if (atlas->TexDesiredWidth > 0)
2491 atlas->TexWidth = atlas->TexDesiredWidth;
2492 else
2493 atlas->TexWidth = (surface_sqrt >= 4096 * 0.7f) ? 4096 : (surface_sqrt >= 2048 * 0.7f) ? 2048 : (surface_sqrt >= 1024 * 0.7f) ? 1024 : 512;
2494
2495 // 5. Start packing
2496 // Pack our extra data rectangles first, so it will be on the upper-left corner of our texture (UV will have small values).
2497 const int TEX_HEIGHT_MAX = 1024 * 32;
2498 stbtt_pack_context spc = {};
2499 stbtt_PackBegin(&spc, NULL, atlas->TexWidth, TEX_HEIGHT_MAX, 0, atlas->TexGlyphPadding, NULL);
2500 ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(atlas, spc.pack_info);
2501
2502 // 6. Pack each source font. No rendering yet, we are working with rectangles in an infinitely tall texture at this point.
2503 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2504 {
2505 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2506 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2507 continue;
2508
2509 stbrp_pack_rects((stbrp_context*)spc.pack_info, src_tmp.Rects, src_tmp.GlyphsCount);
2510
2511 // Extend texture height and mark missing glyphs as non-packed so we won't render them.
2512 // FIXME: We are not handling packing failure here (would happen if we got off TEX_HEIGHT_MAX or if a single if larger than TexWidth?)
2513 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
2514 if (src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].was_packed)
2515 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].y + src_tmp.Rects[glyph_i].h);
2516 }
2517
2518 // 7. Allocate texture
2519 atlas->TexHeight = (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoPowerOfTwoHeight) ? (atlas->TexHeight + 1) : ImUpperPowerOfTwo(atlas->TexHeight);
2520 atlas->TexUvScale = ImVec2(1.0f / atlas->TexWidth, 1.0f / atlas->TexHeight);
2521 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 = (unsigned char*)IM_ALLOC(atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
2522 memset(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, 0, atlas->TexWidth * atlas->TexHeight);
2523 spc.pixels = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8;
2524 spc.height = atlas->TexHeight;
2525
2526 // 8. Render/rasterize font characters into the texture
2527 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2528 {
2529 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2530 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2531 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2532 continue;
2533
2534 stbtt_PackFontRangesRenderIntoRects(&spc, &src_tmp.FontInfo, &src_tmp.PackRange, 1, src_tmp.Rects);
2535
2536 // Apply multiply operator
2537 if (cfg.RasterizerMultiply != 1.0f)
2538 {
2539 unsigned char multiply_table[256];
2540 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyCalcLookupTable(multiply_table, cfg.RasterizerMultiply);
2541 stbrp_rect* r = &src_tmp.Rects[0];
2542 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++, r++)
2543 if (r->was_packed)
2544 ImFontAtlasBuildMultiplyRectAlpha8(multiply_table, atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8, r->x, r->y, r->w, r->h, atlas->TexWidth * 1);
2545 }
2546 src_tmp.Rects = NULL;
2547 }
2548
2549 // End packing
2550 stbtt_PackEnd(&spc);
2551 buf_rects.clear();
2552
2553 // 9. Setup ImFont and glyphs for runtime
2554 for (int src_i = 0; src_i < src_tmp_array.Size; src_i++)
2555 {
2556 ImFontBuildSrcData& src_tmp = src_tmp_array[src_i];
2557 if (src_tmp.GlyphsCount == 0)
2558 continue;
2559
2560 // When merging fonts with MergeMode=true:
2561 // - We can have multiple input fonts writing into a same destination font.
2562 // - dst_font->ConfigData is != from cfg which is our source configuration.
2563 ImFontConfig& cfg = atlas->ConfigData[src_i];
2564 ImFont* dst_font = cfg.DstFont;
2565
2566 const float font_scale = stbtt_ScaleForPixelHeight(&src_tmp.FontInfo, cfg.SizePixels);
2567 int unscaled_ascent, unscaled_descent, unscaled_line_gap;
2568 stbtt_GetFontVMetrics(&src_tmp.FontInfo, &unscaled_ascent, &unscaled_descent, &unscaled_line_gap);
2569
2570 const float ascent = ImFloor(unscaled_ascent * font_scale + ((unscaled_ascent > 0.0f) ? +1 : -1));
2571 const float descent = ImFloor(unscaled_descent * font_scale + ((unscaled_descent > 0.0f) ? +1 : -1));
2572 ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(atlas, dst_font, &cfg, ascent, descent);
2573 const float font_off_x = cfg.GlyphOffset.x;
2574 const float font_off_y = cfg.GlyphOffset.y + IM_ROUND(dst_font->Ascent);
2575
2576 for (int glyph_i = 0; glyph_i < src_tmp.GlyphsCount; glyph_i++)
2577 {
2578 // Register glyph
2579 const int codepoint = src_tmp.GlyphsList[glyph_i];
2580 const stbtt_packedchar& pc = src_tmp.PackedChars[glyph_i];
2581 stbtt_aligned_quad q;
2582 float unused_x = 0.0f, unused_y = 0.0f;
2583 stbtt_GetPackedQuad(src_tmp.PackedChars, atlas->TexWidth, atlas->TexHeight, glyph_i, &unused_x, &unused_y, &q, 0);
2584 dst_font->AddGlyph(&cfg, (ImWchar)codepoint, q.x0 + font_off_x, q.y0 + font_off_y, q.x1 + font_off_x, q.y1 + font_off_y, q.s0, q.t0, q.s1, q.t1, pc.xadvance);
2585 }
2586 }
2587
2588 // Cleanup
2589 src_tmp_array.clear_destruct();
2590
2591 ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(atlas);
2592 return true;
2593}
2594
2595const ImFontBuilderIO* ImFontAtlasGetBuilderForStbTruetype()
2596{
2597 static ImFontBuilderIO io;
2598 io.FontBuilder_Build = ImFontAtlasBuildWithStbTruetype;
2599 return &io;
2600}
2601
2602#endif // IMGUI_ENABLE_STB_TRUETYPE
2603
2604void ImFontAtlasBuildSetupFont(ImFontAtlas* atlas, ImFont* font, ImFontConfig* font_config, float ascent, float descent)
2605{
2606 if (!font_config->MergeMode)
2607 {
2608 font->ClearOutputData();
2609 font->FontSize = font_config->SizePixels;
2610 font->ConfigData = font_config;
2611 font->ConfigDataCount = 0;
2612 font->ContainerAtlas = atlas;
2613 font->Ascent = ascent;
2614 font->Descent = descent;
2615 }
2616 font->ConfigDataCount++;
2617}
2618
2619void ImFontAtlasBuildPackCustomRects(ImFontAtlas* atlas, void* stbrp_context_opaque)
2620{
2621 stbrp_context* pack_context = (stbrp_context*)stbrp_context_opaque;
2622 IM_ASSERT(pack_context != NULL);
2623
2624 ImVector<ImFontAtlasCustomRect>& user_rects = atlas->CustomRects;
2625 IM_ASSERT(user_rects.Size >= 1); // We expect at least the default custom rects to be registered, else something went wrong.
2626
2627 ImVector<stbrp_rect> pack_rects;
2628 pack_rects.resize(user_rects.Size);
2629 memset(pack_rects.Data, 0, (size_t)pack_rects.size_in_bytes());
2630 for (int i = 0; i < user_rects.Size; i++)
2631 {
2632 pack_rects[i].w = user_rects[i].Width;
2633 pack_rects[i].h = user_rects[i].Height;
2634 }
2635 stbrp_pack_rects(pack_context, &pack_rects[0], pack_rects.Size);
2636 for (int i = 0; i < pack_rects.Size; i++)
2637 if (pack_rects[i].was_packed)
2638 {
2639 user_rects[i].X = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].x;
2640 user_rects[i].Y = (unsigned short)pack_rects[i].y;
2641 IM_ASSERT(pack_rects[i].w == user_rects[i].Width && pack_rects[i].h == user_rects[i].Height);
2642 atlas->TexHeight = ImMax(atlas->TexHeight, pack_rects[i].y + pack_rects[i].h);
2643 }
2644}
2645
2646void ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned char in_marker_pixel_value)
2647{
2648 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
2649 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
2650 unsigned char* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
2651 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
2652 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
2653 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : 0x00;
2654}
2655
2656void ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(ImFontAtlas* atlas, int x, int y, int w, int h, const char* in_str, char in_marker_char, unsigned int in_marker_pixel_value)
2657{
2658 IM_ASSERT(x >= 0 && x + w <= atlas->TexWidth);
2659 IM_ASSERT(y >= 0 && y + h <= atlas->TexHeight);
2660 unsigned int* out_pixel = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 + x + (y * atlas->TexWidth);
2661 for (int off_y = 0; off_y < h; off_y++, out_pixel += atlas->TexWidth, in_str += w)
2662 for (int off_x = 0; off_x < w; off_x++)
2663 out_pixel[off_x] = (in_str[off_x] == in_marker_char) ? in_marker_pixel_value : IM_COL32_BLACK_TRANS;
2664}
2665
2666static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2667{
2668 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdMouseCursors);
2669 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
2670
2671 const int w = atlas->TexWidth;
2672 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
2673 {
2674 // Render/copy pixels
2675 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1 && r->Height == FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
2676 const int x_for_white = r->X;
2677 const int x_for_black = r->X + FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W + 1;
2678 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
2679 {
2680 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', 0xFF);
2681 ImFontAtlasBuildRender8bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', 0xFF);
2682 }
2683 else
2684 {
2685 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_white, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, '.', IM_COL32_WHITE);
2686 ImFontAtlasBuildRender32bppRectFromString(atlas, x_for_black, r->Y, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_PIXELS, 'X', IM_COL32_WHITE);
2687 }
2688 }
2689 else
2690 {
2691 // Render 4 white pixels
2692 IM_ASSERT(r->Width == 2 && r->Height == 2);
2693 const int offset = (int)r->X + (int)r->Y * w;
2694 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
2695 {
2696 atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[offset + w + 1] = 0xFF;
2697 }
2698 else
2699 {
2700 atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + 1] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w] = atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[offset + w + 1] = IM_COL32_WHITE;
2701 }
2702 }
2703 atlas->TexUvWhitePixel = ImVec2((r->X + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.x, (r->Y + 0.5f) * atlas->TexUvScale.y);
2704}
2705
2706static void ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2707{
2708 if (atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines)
2709 return;
2710
2711 // This generates a triangular shape in the texture, with the various line widths stacked on top of each other to allow interpolation between them
2712 ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = atlas->GetCustomRectByIndex(atlas->PackIdLines);
2713 IM_ASSERT(r->IsPacked());
2714 for (unsigned int n = 0; n < IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1; n++) // +1 because of the zero-width row
2715 {
2716 // Each line consists of at least two empty pixels at the ends, with a line of solid pixels in the middle
2717 unsigned int y = n;
2718 unsigned int line_width = n;
2719 unsigned int pad_left = (r->Width - line_width) / 2;
2720 unsigned int pad_right = r->Width - (pad_left + line_width);
2721
2722 // Write each slice
2723 IM_ASSERT(pad_left + line_width + pad_right == r->Width && y < r->Height); // Make sure we're inside the texture bounds before we start writing pixels
2724 if (atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL)
2725 {
2726 unsigned char* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
2727 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
2728 *(write_ptr + i) = 0x00;
2729
2730 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
2731 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = 0xFF;
2732
2733 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
2734 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = 0x00;
2735 }
2736 else
2737 {
2738 unsigned int* write_ptr = &atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32[r->X + ((r->Y + y) * atlas->TexWidth)];
2739 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_left; i++)
2740 *(write_ptr + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
2741
2742 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < line_width; i++)
2743 *(write_ptr + pad_left + i) = IM_COL32_WHITE;
2744
2745 for (unsigned int i = 0; i < pad_right; i++)
2746 *(write_ptr + pad_left + line_width + i) = IM_COL32(255, 255, 255, 0);
2747 }
2748
2749 // Calculate UVs for this line
2750 ImVec2 uv0 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left - 1), (float)(r->Y + y)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2751 ImVec2 uv1 = ImVec2((float)(r->X + pad_left + line_width + 1), (float)(r->Y + y + 1)) * atlas->TexUvScale;
2752 float half_v = (uv0.y + uv1.y) * 0.5f; // Calculate a constant V in the middle of the row to avoid sampling artifacts
2753 atlas->TexUvLines[n] = ImVec4(uv0.x, half_v, uv1.x, half_v);
2754 }
2755}
2756
2757// Note: this is called / shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder
2758void ImFontAtlasBuildInit(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2759{
2760 // Register texture region for mouse cursors or standard white pixels
2761 if (atlas->PackIdMouseCursors < 0)
2762 {
2763 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoMouseCursors))
2764 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_W * 2 + 1, FONT_ATLAS_DEFAULT_TEX_DATA_H);
2765 else
2766 atlas->PackIdMouseCursors = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(2, 2);
2767 }
2768
2769 // Register texture region for thick lines
2770 // The +2 here is to give space for the end caps, whilst height +1 is to accommodate the fact we have a zero-width row
2771 if (atlas->PackIdLines < 0)
2772 {
2773 if (!(atlas->Flags & ImFontAtlasFlags_NoBakedLines))
2774 atlas->PackIdLines = atlas->AddCustomRectRegular(IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 2, IM_DRAWLIST_TEX_LINES_WIDTH_MAX + 1);
2775 }
2776}
2777
2778// This is called/shared by both the stb_truetype and the FreeType builder.
2779void ImFontAtlasBuildFinish(ImFontAtlas* atlas)
2780{
2781 // Render into our custom data blocks
2782 IM_ASSERT(atlas->TexPixelsAlpha8 != NULL || atlas->TexPixelsRGBA32 != NULL);
2783 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderDefaultTexData(atlas);
2784 ImFontAtlasBuildRenderLinesTexData(atlas);
2785
2786 // Register custom rectangle glyphs
2787 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->CustomRects.Size; i++)
2788 {
2789 const ImFontAtlasCustomRect* r = &atlas->CustomRects[i];
2790 if (r->Font == NULL || r->GlyphID == 0)
2791 continue;
2792
2793 // Will ignore ImFontConfig settings: GlyphMinAdvanceX, GlyphMinAdvanceY, GlyphExtraSpacing, PixelSnapH
2794 IM_ASSERT(r->Font->ContainerAtlas == atlas);
2795 ImVec2 uv0, uv1;
2796 atlas->CalcCustomRectUV(r, &uv0, &uv1);
2797 r->Font->AddGlyph(NULL, (ImWchar)r->GlyphID, r->GlyphOffset.x, r->GlyphOffset.y, r->GlyphOffset.x + r->Width, r->GlyphOffset.y + r->Height, uv0.x, uv0.y, uv1.x, uv1.y, r->GlyphAdvanceX);
2798 }
2799
2800 // Build all fonts lookup tables
2801 for (int i = 0; i < atlas->Fonts.Size; i++)
2802 if (atlas->Fonts[i]->DirtyLookupTables)
2803 atlas->Fonts[i]->BuildLookupTable();
2804
2805 atlas->TexReady = true;
2806}

2810{
2811 static const ImWchar ranges[] =
2812 {
2813 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
2814 0,
2815 };
2816 return &ranges[0];
2817}

2843const ImWchar* ImFontAtlas::GetGlyphRangesChineseFull()

2848 0x2000, 0x206F, // General Punctuation

2858
2859static void UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(int base_codepoint, const short* accumulative_offsets, int accumulative_offsets_count, ImWchar* out_ranges)
2860{
2861 for (int n = 0; n < accumulative_offsets_count; n++, out_ranges += 2)
2862 {
2863 out_ranges[0] = out_ranges[1] = (ImWchar)(base_codepoint + accumulative_offsets[n]);
2864 base_codepoint += accumulative_offsets[n];
2865 }
2866 out_ranges[0] = 0;
2867}

2923 static ImWchar base_ranges[] = // not zero-terminated
2924 {
2925 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
2926 0x2000, 0x206F, // General Punctuation
2927 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
2928 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
2929 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
2930 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD // Invalid
2931 };
2932 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00) * 2 + 1] = { 0 };
2933 if (!full_ranges[0])
2934 {
2935 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));
2936 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00, IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00), full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
2937 }
2938 return &full_ranges[0];
2939}

3012 3,2,1,1,1,1,2,1,1,
3013 };
3014 static ImWchar base_ranges[] = // not zero-terminated
3015 {
3016 0x0020, 0x00FF, // Basic Latin + Latin Supplement
3017 0x3000, 0x30FF, // CJK Symbols and Punctuations, Hiragana, Katakana
3018 0x31F0, 0x31FF, // Katakana Phonetic Extensions
3019 0xFF00, 0xFFEF, // Half-width characters
3020 0xFFFD, 0xFFFD // Invalid
3021 };
3022 static ImWchar full_ranges[IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges) + IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00)*2 + 1] = { 0 };
3023 if (!full_ranges[0])
3024 {
3025 memcpy(full_ranges, base_ranges, sizeof(base_ranges));
3026 UnpackAccumulativeOffsetsIntoRanges(0x4E00, accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00, IM_ARRAYSIZE(accumulative_offsets_from_0x4E00), full_ranges + IM_ARRAYSIZE(base_ranges));
3027 }
3028 return &full_ranges[0];
3029}

3073//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3074// [SECTION] ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder
3075//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3076
3077void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddText(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3078{
3079 while (text_end ? (text < text_end) : *text)
3080 {
3081 unsigned int c = 0;
3082 int c_len = ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, text, text_end);
3083 text += c_len;
3084 if (c_len == 0)
3085 break;
3086 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3087 }
3088}
3089
3090void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::AddRanges(const ImWchar* ranges)
3091{
3092 for (; ranges[0]; ranges += 2)
3093 for (unsigned int c = ranges[0]; c <= ranges[1] && c <= IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX; c++) //-V560
3094 AddChar((ImWchar)c);
3095}
3096
3097void ImFontGlyphRangesBuilder::BuildRanges(ImVector<ImWchar>* out_ranges)
3098{
3099 const int max_codepoint = IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_MAX;
3100 for (int n = 0; n <= max_codepoint; n++)
3101 if (GetBit(n))
3102 {
3103 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3104 while (n < max_codepoint && GetBit(n + 1))
3105 n++;
3106 out_ranges->push_back((ImWchar)n);
3107 }
3108 out_ranges->push_back(0);
3109}

3114
3115ImFont::ImFont()
3116{
3117 FontSize = 0.0f;
3118 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
3119 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)-1;
3120 EllipsisChar = (ImWchar)-1;
3121 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = 0.0f;
3122 EllipsisCharCount = 0;
3123 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
3124 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
3125 ConfigData = NULL;
3126 ConfigDataCount = 0;
3127 DirtyLookupTables = false;
3128 Scale = 1.0f;
3129 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
3130 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
3131 memset(Used4kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used4kPagesMap));
3132}

3134ImFont::~ImFont()

3138
3139void ImFont::ClearOutputData()
3140{
3141 FontSize = 0.0f;
3142 FallbackAdvanceX = 0.0f;
3143 Glyphs.clear();
3144 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3145 IndexLookup.clear();
3146 FallbackGlyph = NULL;
3147 ContainerAtlas = NULL;
3148 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3149 Ascent = Descent = 0.0f;
3150 MetricsTotalSurface = 0;
3151}
3152
3153static ImWchar FindFirstExistingGlyph(ImFont* font, const ImWchar* candidate_chars, int candidate_chars_count)
3154{
3155 for (int n = 0; n < candidate_chars_count; n++)
3156 if (font->FindGlyphNoFallback(candidate_chars[n]) != NULL)
3157 return candidate_chars[n];
3158 return (ImWchar)-1;
3159}
3160
3161void ImFont::BuildLookupTable()
3162{
3163 int max_codepoint = 0;
3164 for (int i = 0; i != Glyphs.Size; i++)
3165 max_codepoint = ImMax(max_codepoint, (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint);
3166
3167 // Build lookup table
3168 IM_ASSERT(Glyphs.Size < 0xFFFF); // -1 is reserved
3169 IndexAdvanceX.clear();
3170 IndexLookup.clear();
3171 DirtyLookupTables = false;
3172 memset(Used4kPagesMap, 0, sizeof(Used4kPagesMap));
3173 GrowIndex(max_codepoint + 1);
3174 for (int i = 0; i < Glyphs.Size; i++)
3175 {
3176 int codepoint = (int)Glyphs[i].Codepoint;
3177 IndexAdvanceX[codepoint] = Glyphs[i].AdvanceX;
3178 IndexLookup[codepoint] = (ImWchar)i;
3179
3180 // Mark 4K page as used
3181 const int page_n = codepoint / 4096;
3182 Used4kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] |= 1 << (page_n & 7);
3183 }
3184
3185 // Create a glyph to handle TAB
3186 // FIXME: Needs proper TAB handling but it needs to be contextualized (or we could arbitrary say that each string starts at "column 0" ?)
3187 if (FindGlyph((ImWchar)' '))
3188 {
3189 if (Glyphs.back().Codepoint != '\t') // So we can call this function multiple times (FIXME: Flaky)
3190 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3191 ImFontGlyph& tab_glyph = Glyphs.back();
3192 tab_glyph = *FindGlyph((ImWchar)' ');
3193 tab_glyph.Codepoint = '\t';
3194 tab_glyph.AdvanceX *= IM_TABSIZE;
3195 IndexAdvanceX[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (float)tab_glyph.AdvanceX;
3196 IndexLookup[(int)tab_glyph.Codepoint] = (ImWchar)(Glyphs.Size - 1);
3197 }
3198
3199 // Mark special glyphs as not visible (note that AddGlyph already mark as non-visible glyphs with zero-size polygons)
3200 SetGlyphVisible((ImWchar)' ', false);
3201 SetGlyphVisible((ImWchar)'\t', false);
3202
3203 // Ellipsis character is required for rendering elided text. We prefer using U+2026 (horizontal ellipsis).
3204 // However some old fonts may contain ellipsis at U+0085. Here we auto-detect most suitable ellipsis character.
3205 // FIXME: Note that 0x2026 is rarely included in our font ranges. Because of this we are more likely to use three individual dots.
3206 const ImWchar ellipsis_chars[] = { (ImWchar)0x2026, (ImWchar)0x0085 };
3207 const ImWchar dots_chars[] = { (ImWchar)'.', (ImWchar)0xFF0E };
3208 if (EllipsisChar == (ImWchar)-1)
3209 EllipsisChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, ellipsis_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(ellipsis_chars));
3210 const ImWchar dot_char = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, dots_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(dots_chars));
3211 if (EllipsisChar != (ImWchar)-1)
3212 {
3213 EllipsisCharCount = 1;
3214 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep = FindGlyph(EllipsisChar)->X1;
3215 }
3216 else if (dot_char != (ImWchar)-1)
3217 {
3218 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph(dot_char);
3219 EllipsisChar = dot_char;
3220 EllipsisCharCount = 3;
3221 EllipsisCharStep = (glyph->X1 - glyph->X0) + 1.0f;
3222 EllipsisWidth = EllipsisCharStep * 3.0f - 1.0f;
3223 }
3224
3225 // Setup fallback character
3226 const ImWchar fallback_chars[] = { (ImWchar)IM_UNICODE_CODEPOINT_INVALID, (ImWchar)'?', (ImWchar)' ' };
3227 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3228 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3229 {
3230 FallbackChar = FindFirstExistingGlyph(this, fallback_chars, IM_ARRAYSIZE(fallback_chars));
3231 FallbackGlyph = FindGlyphNoFallback(FallbackChar);
3232 if (FallbackGlyph == NULL)
3233 {
3234 FallbackGlyph = &Glyphs.back();
3235 FallbackChar = (ImWchar)FallbackGlyph->Codepoint;
3236 }
3237 }
3238
3239 FallbackAdvanceX = FallbackGlyph->AdvanceX;
3240 for (int i = 0; i < max_codepoint + 1; i++)
3241 if (IndexAdvanceX[i] < 0.0f)
3242 IndexAdvanceX[i] = FallbackAdvanceX;
3243}
3244
3245// API is designed this way to avoid exposing the 4K page size
3246// e.g. use with IsGlyphRangeUnused(0, 255)
3247bool ImFont::IsGlyphRangeUnused(unsigned int c_begin, unsigned int c_last)
3248{
3249 unsigned int page_begin = (c_begin / 4096);
3250 unsigned int page_last = (c_last / 4096);
3251 for (unsigned int page_n = page_begin; page_n <= page_last; page_n++)
3252 if ((page_n >> 3) < sizeof(Used4kPagesMap))
3253 if (Used4kPagesMap[page_n >> 3] & (1 << (page_n & 7)))
3254 return false;
3255 return true;
3256}
3257
3258void ImFont::SetGlyphVisible(ImWchar c, bool visible)
3259{
3260 if (ImFontGlyph* glyph = (ImFontGlyph*)(void*)FindGlyph((ImWchar)c))
3261 glyph->Visible = visible ? 1 : 0;
3262}
3263
3264void ImFont::GrowIndex(int new_size)
3265{
3266 IM_ASSERT(IndexAdvanceX.Size == IndexLookup.Size);
3267 if (new_size <= IndexLookup.Size)
3268 return;
3269 IndexAdvanceX.resize(new_size, -1.0f);
3270 IndexLookup.resize(new_size, (ImWchar)-1);
3271}
3272
3273// x0/y0/x1/y1 are offset from the character upper-left layout position, in pixels. Therefore x0/y0 are often fairly close to zero.
3274// Not to be mistaken with texture coordinates, which are held by u0/v0/u1/v1 in normalized format (0.0..1.0 on each texture axis).
3275// 'cfg' is not necessarily == 'this->ConfigData' because multiple source fonts+configs can be used to build one target font.
3276void ImFont::AddGlyph(const ImFontConfig* cfg, ImWchar codepoint, float x0, float y0, float x1, float y1, float u0, float v0, float u1, float v1, float advance_x)
3277{
3278 if (cfg != NULL)
3279 {
3280 // Clamp & recenter if needed
3281 const float advance_x_original = advance_x;
3282 advance_x = ImClamp(advance_x, cfg->GlyphMinAdvanceX, cfg->GlyphMaxAdvanceX);
3283 if (advance_x != advance_x_original)
3284 {
3285 float char_off_x = cfg->PixelSnapH ? ImFloor((advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f) : (advance_x - advance_x_original) * 0.5f;
3286 x0 += char_off_x;
3287 x1 += char_off_x;
3288 }
3289
3290 // Snap to pixel
3291 if (cfg->PixelSnapH)
3292 advance_x = IM_ROUND(advance_x);
3293
3294 // Bake spacing
3295 advance_x += cfg->GlyphExtraSpacing.x;
3296 }
3297
3298 Glyphs.resize(Glyphs.Size + 1);
3299 ImFontGlyph& glyph = Glyphs.back();
3300 glyph.Codepoint = (unsigned int)codepoint;
3301 glyph.Visible = (x0 != x1) && (y0 != y1);
3302 glyph.Colored = false;
3303 glyph.X0 = x0;
3304 glyph.Y0 = y0;
3305 glyph.X1 = x1;
3306 glyph.Y1 = y1;
3307 glyph.U0 = u0;
3308 glyph.V0 = v0;
3309 glyph.U1 = u1;
3310 glyph.V1 = v1;
3311 glyph.AdvanceX = advance_x;
3312
3313 // Compute rough surface usage metrics (+1 to account for average padding, +0.99 to round)
3314 // We use (U1-U0)*TexWidth instead of X1-X0 to account for oversampling.
3315 float pad = ContainerAtlas->TexGlyphPadding + 0.99f;
3316 DirtyLookupTables = true;
3317 MetricsTotalSurface += (int)((glyph.U1 - glyph.U0) * ContainerAtlas->TexWidth + pad) * (int)((glyph.V1 - glyph.V0) * ContainerAtlas->TexHeight + pad);
3318}
3319
3320void ImFont::AddRemapChar(ImWchar dst, ImWchar src, bool overwrite_dst)
3321{
3322 IM_ASSERT(IndexLookup.Size > 0); // Currently this can only be called AFTER the font has been built, aka after calling ImFontAtlas::GetTexDataAs*() function.
3323 unsigned int index_size = (unsigned int)IndexLookup.Size;
3324
3325 if (dst < index_size && IndexLookup.Data[dst] == (ImWchar)-1 && !overwrite_dst) // 'dst' already exists
3326 return;
3327 if (src >= index_size && dst >= index_size) // both 'dst' and 'src' don't exist -> no-op
3328 return;
3329
3330 GrowIndex(dst + 1);
3331 IndexLookup[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexLookup.Data[src] : (ImWchar)-1;
3332 IndexAdvanceX[dst] = (src < index_size) ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[src] : 1.0f;
3333}
3334
3335const ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyph(ImWchar c) const
3336{
3337 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3338 return FallbackGlyph;
3339 const ImWchar i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3340 if (i == (ImWchar)-1)
3341 return FallbackGlyph;
3342 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3343}
3344
3345const ImFontGlyph* ImFont::FindGlyphNoFallback(ImWchar c) const
3346{
3347 if (c >= (size_t)IndexLookup.Size)
3348 return NULL;
3349 const ImWchar i = IndexLookup.Data[c];
3350 if (i == (ImWchar)-1)
3351 return NULL;
3352 return &Glyphs.Data[i];
3353}
3354
3355// Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
3356static inline const char* CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(const char* text, const char* text_end)
3357{
3358 while (text < text_end && ImCharIsBlankA(*text))
3359 text++;
3360 if (*text == '\n')
3361 text++;
3362 return text;
3363}
3364
3365// Simple word-wrapping for English, not full-featured. Please submit failing cases!
3366// This will return the next location to wrap from. If no wrapping if necessary, this will fast-forward to e.g. text_end.
3367// FIXME: Much possible improvements (don't cut things like "word !", "word!!!" but cut within "word,,,,", more sensible support for punctuations, support for Unicode punctuations, etc.)
3368const char* ImFont::CalcWordWrapPositionA(float scale, const char* text, const char* text_end, float wrap_width) const
3369{
3370 // For references, possible wrap point marked with ^
3371 // "aaa bbb, ccc,ddd. eee fff. ggg!"
3372 // ^ ^ ^ ^ ^__ ^ ^
3373
3374 // List of hardcoded separators: .,;!?'"
3375
3376 // Skip extra blanks after a line returns (that includes not counting them in width computation)
3377 // e.g. "Hello world" --> "Hello" "World"
3378
3379 // Cut words that cannot possibly fit within one line.
3380 // e.g.: "The tropical fish" with ~5 characters worth of width --> "The tr" "opical" "fish"
3381 float line_width = 0.0f;
3382 float word_width = 0.0f;
3383 float blank_width = 0.0f;
3384 wrap_width /= scale; // We work with unscaled widths to avoid scaling every characters
3385
3386 const char* word_end = text;
3387 const char* prev_word_end = NULL;
3388 bool inside_word = true;
3389
3390 const char* s = text;
3391 IM_ASSERT(text_end != NULL);
3392 while (s < text_end)
3393 {
3394 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3395 const char* next_s;
3396 if (c < 0x80)
3397 next_s = s + 1;
3398 else
3399 next_s = s + ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3400
3401 if (c < 32)
3402 {
3403 if (c == '\n')
3404 {
3405 line_width = word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
3406 inside_word = true;
3407 s = next_s;
3408 continue;
3409 }
3410 if (c == '\r')
3411 {
3412 s = next_s;
3413 continue;
3414 }
3415 }
3416
3417 const float char_width = ((int)c < IndexAdvanceX.Size ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[c] : FallbackAdvanceX);
3418 if (ImCharIsBlankW(c))
3419 {
3420 if (inside_word)
3421 {
3422 line_width += blank_width;
3423 blank_width = 0.0f;
3424 word_end = s;
3425 }
3426 blank_width += char_width;
3427 inside_word = false;
3428 }
3429 else
3430 {
3431 word_width += char_width;
3432 if (inside_word)
3433 {
3434 word_end = next_s;
3435 }
3436 else
3437 {
3438 prev_word_end = word_end;
3439 line_width += word_width + blank_width;
3440 word_width = blank_width = 0.0f;
3441 }
3442
3443 // Allow wrapping after punctuation.
3444 inside_word = (c != '.' && c != ',' && c != ';' && c != '!' && c != '?' && c != '\"');
3445 }
3446
3447 // We ignore blank width at the end of the line (they can be skipped)
3448 if (line_width + word_width > wrap_width)
3449 {
3450 // Words that cannot possibly fit within an entire line will be cut anywhere.
3451 if (word_width < wrap_width)
3452 s = prev_word_end ? prev_word_end : word_end;
3453 break;
3454 }
3455
3456 s = next_s;
3457 }
3458
3459 // Wrap_width is too small to fit anything. Force displaying 1 character to minimize the height discontinuity.
3460 // +1 may not be a character start point in UTF-8 but it's ok because caller loops use (text >= word_wrap_eol).
3461 if (s == text && text < text_end)
3462 return s + 1;
3463 return s;
3464}
3465
3466ImVec2 ImFont::CalcTextSizeA(float size, float max_width, float wrap_width, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, const char** remaining) const
3467{
3468 if (!text_end)
3469 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin); // FIXME-OPT: Need to avoid this.
3470
3471 const float line_height = size;
3472 const float scale = size / FontSize;
3473
3474 ImVec2 text_size = ImVec2(0, 0);
3475 float line_width = 0.0f;
3476
3477 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
3478 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3479
3480 const char* s = text_begin;
3481 while (s < text_end)
3482 {
3483 if (word_wrap_enabled)
3484 {
3485 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
3486 if (!word_wrap_eol)
3487 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - line_width);
3488
3489 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
3490 {
3491 if (text_size.x < line_width)
3492 text_size.x = line_width;
3493 text_size.y += line_height;
3494 line_width = 0.0f;
3495 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3496 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
3497 continue;
3498 }
3499 }
3500
3501 // Decode and advance source
3502 const char* prev_s = s;
3503 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3504 if (c < 0x80)
3505 s += 1;
3506 else
3507 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3508
3509 if (c < 32)
3510 {
3511 if (c == '\n')
3512 {
3513 text_size.x = ImMax(text_size.x, line_width);
3514 text_size.y += line_height;
3515 line_width = 0.0f;
3516 continue;
3517 }
3518 if (c == '\r')
3519 continue;
3520 }
3521
3522 const float char_width = ((int)c < IndexAdvanceX.Size ? IndexAdvanceX.Data[c] : FallbackAdvanceX) * scale;
3523 if (line_width + char_width >= max_width)
3524 {
3525 s = prev_s;
3526 break;
3527 }
3528
3529 line_width += char_width;
3530 }
3531
3532 if (text_size.x < line_width)
3533 text_size.x = line_width;
3534
3535 if (line_width > 0 || text_size.y == 0.0f)
3536 text_size.y += line_height;
3537
3538 if (remaining)
3539 *remaining = s;
3540
3541 return text_size;
3542}
3543
3544// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
3545void ImFont::RenderChar(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, ImWchar c) const
3546{
3547 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph(c);
3548 if (!glyph || !glyph->Visible)
3549 return;
3550 if (glyph->Colored)
3551 col |= ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
3552 float scale = (size >= 0.0f) ? (size / FontSize) : 1.0f;
3553 float x = IM_FLOOR(pos.x);
3554 float y = IM_FLOOR(pos.y);
3555 draw_list->PrimReserve(6, 4);
3556 draw_list->PrimRectUV(ImVec2(x + glyph->X0 * scale, y + glyph->Y0 * scale), ImVec2(x + glyph->X1 * scale, y + glyph->Y1 * scale), ImVec2(glyph->U0, glyph->V0), ImVec2(glyph->U1, glyph->V1), col);
3557}
3558
3559// Note: as with every ImDrawList drawing function, this expects that the font atlas texture is bound.
3560void ImFont::RenderText(ImDrawList* draw_list, float size, const ImVec2& pos, ImU32 col, const ImVec4& clip_rect, const char* text_begin, const char* text_end, float wrap_width, bool cpu_fine_clip) const
3561{
3562 if (!text_end)
3563 text_end = text_begin + strlen(text_begin); // ImGui:: functions generally already provides a valid text_end, so this is merely to handle direct calls.
3564
3565 // Align to be pixel perfect
3566 float x = IM_FLOOR(pos.x);
3567 float y = IM_FLOOR(pos.y);
3568 if (y > clip_rect.w)
3569 return;
3570
3571 const float start_x = x;
3572 const float scale = size / FontSize;
3573 const float line_height = FontSize * scale;
3574 const bool word_wrap_enabled = (wrap_width > 0.0f);
3575
3576 // Fast-forward to first visible line
3577 const char* s = text_begin;
3578 if (y + line_height < clip_rect.y)
3579 while (y + line_height < clip_rect.y && s < text_end)
3580 {
3581 const char* line_end = (const char*)memchr(s, '\n', text_end - s);
3582 if (word_wrap_enabled)
3583 {
3584 // FIXME-OPT: This is not optimal as do first do a search for \n before calling CalcWordWrapPositionA().
3585 // If the specs for CalcWordWrapPositionA() were reworked to optionally return on \n we could combine both.
3586 // However it is still better than nothing performing the fast-forward!
3587 s = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, line_end ? line_end : text_end, wrap_width);
3588 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end);
3589 }
3590 else
3591 {
3592 s = line_end ? line_end + 1 : text_end;
3593 }
3594 y += line_height;
3595 }
3596
3597 // For large text, scan for the last visible line in order to avoid over-reserving in the call to PrimReserve()
3598 // Note that very large horizontal line will still be affected by the issue (e.g. a one megabyte string buffer without a newline will likely crash atm)
3599 if (text_end - s > 10000 && !word_wrap_enabled)
3600 {
3601 const char* s_end = s;
3602 float y_end = y;
3603 while (y_end < clip_rect.w && s_end < text_end)
3604 {
3605 s_end = (const char*)memchr(s_end, '\n', text_end - s_end);
3606 s_end = s_end ? s_end + 1 : text_end;
3607 y_end += line_height;
3608 }
3609 text_end = s_end;
3610 }
3611 if (s == text_end)
3612 return;
3613
3614 // Reserve vertices for remaining worse case (over-reserving is useful and easily amortized)
3615 const int vtx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 4;
3616 const int idx_count_max = (int)(text_end - s) * 6;
3617 const int idx_expected_size = draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size + idx_count_max;
3618 draw_list->PrimReserve(idx_count_max, vtx_count_max);
3619 ImDrawVert* vtx_write = draw_list->_VtxWritePtr;
3620 ImDrawIdx* idx_write = draw_list->_IdxWritePtr;
3621 unsigned int vtx_index = draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx;
3622
3623 const ImU32 col_untinted = col | ~IM_COL32_A_MASK;
3624 const char* word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3625
3626 while (s < text_end)
3627 {
3628 if (word_wrap_enabled)
3629 {
3630 // Calculate how far we can render. Requires two passes on the string data but keeps the code simple and not intrusive for what's essentially an uncommon feature.
3631 if (!word_wrap_eol)
3632 word_wrap_eol = CalcWordWrapPositionA(scale, s, text_end, wrap_width - (x - start_x));
3633
3634 if (s >= word_wrap_eol)
3635 {
3636 x = start_x;
3637 y += line_height;
3638 word_wrap_eol = NULL;
3639 s = CalcWordWrapNextLineStartA(s, text_end); // Wrapping skips upcoming blanks
3640 continue;
3641 }
3642 }
3643
3644 // Decode and advance source
3645 unsigned int c = (unsigned int)*s;
3646 if (c < 0x80)
3647 s += 1;
3648 else
3649 s += ImTextCharFromUtf8(&c, s, text_end);
3650
3651 if (c < 32)
3652 {
3653 if (c == '\n')
3654 {
3655 x = start_x;
3656 y += line_height;
3657 if (y > clip_rect.w)
3658 break; // break out of main loop
3659 continue;
3660 }
3661 if (c == '\r')
3662 continue;
3663 }
3664
3665 const ImFontGlyph* glyph = FindGlyph((ImWchar)c);
3666 if (glyph == NULL)
3667 continue;
3668
3669 float char_width = glyph->AdvanceX * scale;
3670 if (glyph->Visible)
3671 {
3672 // We don't do a second finer clipping test on the Y axis as we've already skipped anything before clip_rect.y and exit once we pass clip_rect.w
3673 float x1 = x + glyph->X0 * scale;
3674 float x2 = x + glyph->X1 * scale;
3675 float y1 = y + glyph->Y0 * scale;
3676 float y2 = y + glyph->Y1 * scale;
3677 if (x1 <= clip_rect.z && x2 >= clip_rect.x)
3678 {
3679 // Render a character
3680 float u1 = glyph->U0;
3681 float v1 = glyph->V0;
3682 float u2 = glyph->U1;
3683 float v2 = glyph->V1;
3684
3685 // CPU side clipping used to fit text in their frame when the frame is too small. Only does clipping for axis aligned quads.
3686 if (cpu_fine_clip)
3687 {
3688 if (x1 < clip_rect.x)
3689 {
3690 u1 = u1 + (1.0f - (x2 - clip_rect.x) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
3691 x1 = clip_rect.x;
3692 }
3693 if (y1 < clip_rect.y)
3694 {
3695 v1 = v1 + (1.0f - (y2 - clip_rect.y) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
3696 y1 = clip_rect.y;
3697 }
3698 if (x2 > clip_rect.z)
3699 {
3700 u2 = u1 + ((clip_rect.z - x1) / (x2 - x1)) * (u2 - u1);
3701 x2 = clip_rect.z;
3702 }
3703 if (y2 > clip_rect.w)
3704 {
3705 v2 = v1 + ((clip_rect.w - y1) / (y2 - y1)) * (v2 - v1);
3706 y2 = clip_rect.w;
3707 }
3708 if (y1 >= y2)
3709 {
3710 x += char_width;
3711 continue;
3712 }
3713 }
3714
3715 // Support for untinted glyphs
3716 ImU32 glyph_col = glyph->Colored ? col_untinted : col;
3717
3718 // We are NOT calling PrimRectUV() here because non-inlined causes too much overhead in a debug builds. Inlined here:
3719 {
3720 vtx_write[0].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[0].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[0].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[0].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[0].uv.y = v1;
3721 vtx_write[1].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[1].pos.y = y1; vtx_write[1].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[1].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[1].uv.y = v1;
3722 vtx_write[2].pos.x = x2; vtx_write[2].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[2].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[2].uv.x = u2; vtx_write[2].uv.y = v2;
3723 vtx_write[3].pos.x = x1; vtx_write[3].pos.y = y2; vtx_write[3].col = glyph_col; vtx_write[3].uv.x = u1; vtx_write[3].uv.y = v2;
3724 idx_write[0] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[1] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 1); idx_write[2] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2);
3725 idx_write[3] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index); idx_write[4] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 2); idx_write[5] = (ImDrawIdx)(vtx_index + 3);
3726 vtx_write += 4;
3727 vtx_index += 4;
3728 idx_write += 6;
3729 }
3730 }
3731 }
3732 x += char_width;
3733 }
3734
3735 // Give back unused vertices (clipped ones, blanks) ~ this is essentially a PrimUnreserve() action.
3736 draw_list->VtxBuffer.Size = (int)(vtx_write - draw_list->VtxBuffer.Data); // Same as calling shrink()
3737 draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size = (int)(idx_write - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Data);
3738 draw_list->CmdBuffer[draw_list->CmdBuffer.Size - 1].ElemCount -= (idx_expected_size - draw_list->IdxBuffer.Size);
3739 draw_list->_VtxWritePtr = vtx_write;
3740 draw_list->_IdxWritePtr = idx_write;
3741 draw_list->_VtxCurrentIdx = vtx_index;
3742}

3744//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3745// [SECTION] ImGui Internal Render Helpers
3746//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3747// Vaguely redesigned to stop accessing ImGui global state:
3748// - RenderArrow()
3749// - RenderBullet()
3750// - RenderCheckMark()
3751// - RenderArrowPointingAt()
3752// - RenderRectFilledRangeH()
3753// - RenderRectFilledWithHole()
3754//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3755// Function in need of a redesign (legacy mess)
3756// - RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard()
3757//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3758
3759// Render an arrow aimed to be aligned with text (p_min is a position in the same space text would be positioned). To e.g. denote expanded/collapsed state
3760void ImGui::RenderArrow(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, ImGuiDir dir, float scale)
3761{
3762 const float h = draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 1.00f;
3763 float r = h * 0.40f * scale;
3764 ImVec2 center = pos + ImVec2(h * 0.50f, h * 0.50f * scale);
3765
3766 ImVec2 a, b, c;
3767 switch (dir)
3768 {
3769 case ImGuiDir_Up:
3770 case ImGuiDir_Down:
3771 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Up) r = -r;
3772 a = ImVec2(+0.000f, +0.750f) * r;
3773 b = ImVec2(-0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
3774 c = ImVec2(+0.866f, -0.750f) * r;
3775 break;
3776 case ImGuiDir_Left:
3777 case ImGuiDir_Right:
3778 if (dir == ImGuiDir_Left) r = -r;
3779 a = ImVec2(+0.750f, +0.000f) * r;
3780 b = ImVec2(-0.750f, +0.866f) * r;
3781 c = ImVec2(-0.750f, -0.866f) * r;
3782 break;
3783 case ImGuiDir_None:
3784 case ImGuiDir_COUNT:
3785 IM_ASSERT(0);
3786 break;
3787 }
3788 draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(center + a, center + b, center + c, col);
3789}
3790
3791void ImGui::RenderBullet(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col)
3792{
3793 // FIXME-OPT: This should be baked in font.
3794 draw_list->AddCircleFilled(pos, draw_list->_Data->FontSize * 0.20f, col, 8);
3795}
3796
3797void ImGui::RenderCheckMark(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImU32 col, float sz)
3798{
3799 float thickness = ImMax(sz / 5.0f, 1.0f);
3800 sz -= thickness * 0.5f;
3801 pos += ImVec2(thickness * 0.25f, thickness * 0.25f);
3802
3803 float third = sz / 3.0f;
3804 float bx = pos.x + third;
3805 float by = pos.y + sz - third * 0.5f;
3806 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx - third, by - third));
3807 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx, by));
3808 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(bx + third * 2.0f, by - third * 2.0f));
3809 draw_list->PathStroke(col, 0, thickness);
3810}
3811
3812// Render an arrow. 'pos' is position of the arrow tip. half_sz.x is length from base to tip. half_sz.y is length on each side.
3813void ImGui::RenderArrowPointingAt(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 pos, ImVec2 half_sz, ImGuiDir direction, ImU32 col)
3814{
3815 switch (direction)
3816 {
3817 case ImGuiDir_Left: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
3818 case ImGuiDir_Right: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
3819 case ImGuiDir_Up: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y + half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
3820 case ImGuiDir_Down: draw_list->AddTriangleFilled(ImVec2(pos.x - half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), ImVec2(pos.x + half_sz.x, pos.y - half_sz.y), pos, col); return;
3821 case ImGuiDir_None: case ImGuiDir_COUNT: break; // Fix warnings
3822 }
3823}
3824
3825static inline float ImAcos01(float x)
3826{
3827 if (x <= 0.0f) return IM_PI * 0.5f;
3828 if (x >= 1.0f) return 0.0f;
3829 return ImAcos(x);
3830 //return (-0.69813170079773212f * x * x - 0.87266462599716477f) * x + 1.5707963267948966f; // Cheap approximation, may be enough for what we do.
3831}
3832
3833// FIXME: Cleanup and move code to ImDrawList.
3834void ImGui::RenderRectFilledRangeH(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& rect, ImU32 col, float x_start_norm, float x_end_norm, float rounding)
3835{
3836 if (x_end_norm == x_start_norm)
3837 return;
3838 if (x_start_norm > x_end_norm)
3839 ImSwap(x_start_norm, x_end_norm);
3840
3841 ImVec2 p0 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_start_norm), rect.Min.y);
3842 ImVec2 p1 = ImVec2(ImLerp(rect.Min.x, rect.Max.x, x_end_norm), rect.Max.y);
3843 if (rounding == 0.0f)
3844 {
3845 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p0, p1, col, 0.0f);
3846 return;
3847 }
3848
3849 rounding = ImClamp(ImMin((rect.Max.x - rect.Min.x) * 0.5f, (rect.Max.y - rect.Min.y) * 0.5f) - 1.0f, 0.0f, rounding);
3850 const float inv_rounding = 1.0f / rounding;
3851 const float arc0_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p0.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
3852 const float arc0_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (p1.x - rect.Min.x) * inv_rounding);
3853 const float half_pi = IM_PI * 0.5f; // We will == compare to this because we know this is the exact value ImAcos01 can return.
3854 const float x0 = ImMax(p0.x, rect.Min.x + rounding);
3855 if (arc0_b == arc0_e)
3856 {
3857 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y));
3858 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y));
3859 }
3860 else if (arc0_b == 0.0f && arc0_e == half_pi)
3861 {
3862 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 3, 6); // BL
3863 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 6, 9); // TR
3864 }
3865 else
3866 {
3867 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p1.y - rounding), rounding, IM_PI - arc0_e, IM_PI - arc0_b, 3); // BL
3868 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x0, p0.y + rounding), rounding, IM_PI + arc0_b, IM_PI + arc0_e, 3); // TR
3869 }
3870 if (p1.x > rect.Min.x + rounding)
3871 {
3872 const float arc1_b = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p1.x) * inv_rounding);
3873 const float arc1_e = ImAcos01(1.0f - (rect.Max.x - p0.x) * inv_rounding);
3874 const float x1 = ImMin(p1.x, rect.Max.x - rounding);
3875 if (arc1_b == arc1_e)
3876 {
3877 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y));
3878 draw_list->PathLineTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y));
3879 }
3880 else if (arc1_b == 0.0f && arc1_e == half_pi)
3881 {
3882 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, 9, 12); // TR
3883 draw_list->PathArcToFast(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, 0, 3); // BR
3884 }
3885 else
3886 {
3887 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p0.y + rounding), rounding, -arc1_e, -arc1_b, 3); // TR
3888 draw_list->PathArcTo(ImVec2(x1, p1.y - rounding), rounding, +arc1_b, +arc1_e, 3); // BR
3889 }
3890 }
3891 draw_list->PathFillConvex(col);
3892}
3893
3894void ImGui::RenderRectFilledWithHole(ImDrawList* draw_list, const ImRect& outer, const ImRect& inner, ImU32 col, float rounding)
3895{
3896 const bool fill_L = (inner.Min.x > outer.Min.x);
3897 const bool fill_R = (inner.Max.x < outer.Max.x);
3898 const bool fill_U = (inner.Min.y > outer.Min.y);
3899 const bool fill_D = (inner.Max.y < outer.Max.y);
3900 if (fill_L) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft));
3901 if (fill_R) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_U ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight) | (fill_D ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
3902 if (fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight));
3903 if (fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone | (fill_L ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft) | (fill_R ? 0 : ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight));
3904 if (fill_L && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft);
3905 if (fill_R && fill_U) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, outer.Min.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, inner.Min.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight);
3906 if (fill_L && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(outer.Min.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(inner.Min.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft);
3907 if (fill_R && fill_D) draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(inner.Max.x, inner.Max.y), ImVec2(outer.Max.x, outer.Max.y), col, rounding, ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight);
3908}
3909
3910// Helper for ColorPicker4()
3911// NB: This is rather brittle and will show artifact when rounding this enabled if rounded corners overlap multiple cells. Caller currently responsible for avoiding that.
3912// Spent a non reasonable amount of time trying to getting this right for ColorButton with rounding+anti-aliasing+ImGuiColorEditFlags_HalfAlphaPreview flag + various grid sizes and offsets, and eventually gave up... probably more reasonable to disable rounding altogether.
3913// FIXME: uses ImGui::GetColorU32
3914void ImGui::RenderColorRectWithAlphaCheckerboard(ImDrawList* draw_list, ImVec2 p_min, ImVec2 p_max, ImU32 col, float grid_step, ImVec2 grid_off, float rounding, ImDrawFlags flags)
3915{
3916 if ((flags & ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersMask_) == 0)
3917 flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersDefault_;
3918 if (((col & IM_COL32_A_MASK) >> IM_COL32_A_SHIFT) < 0xFF)
3919 {
3920 ImU32 col_bg1 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(204, 204, 204, 255), col));
3921 ImU32 col_bg2 = GetColorU32(ImAlphaBlendColors(IM_COL32(128, 128, 128, 255), col));
3922 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col_bg1, rounding, flags);
3923
3924 int yi = 0;
3925 for (float y = p_min.y + grid_off.y; y < p_max.y; y += grid_step, yi++)
3926 {
3927 float y1 = ImClamp(y, p_min.y, p_max.y), y2 = ImMin(y + grid_step, p_max.y);
3928 if (y2 <= y1)
3929 continue;
3930 for (float x = p_min.x + grid_off.x + (yi & 1) * grid_step; x < p_max.x; x += grid_step * 2.0f)
3931 {
3932 float x1 = ImClamp(x, p_min.x, p_max.x), x2 = ImMin(x + grid_step, p_max.x);
3933 if (x2 <= x1)
3934 continue;
3935 ImDrawFlags cell_flags = ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone;
3936 if (y1 <= p_min.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersTopRight; }
3937 if (y2 >= p_max.y) { if (x1 <= p_min.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomLeft; if (x2 >= p_max.x) cell_flags |= ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersBottomRight; }
3938
3939 // Combine flags
3940 cell_flags = (flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone || cell_flags == ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone) ? ImDrawFlags_RoundCornersNone : (cell_flags & flags);
3941 draw_list->AddRectFilled(ImVec2(x1, y1), ImVec2(x2, y2), col_bg2, rounding, cell_flags);
3942 }
3943 }
3944 }
3945 else
3946 {
3947 draw_list->AddRectFilled(p_min, p_max, col, rounding, flags);
3948 }
3949}
3950
3951//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3952// [SECTION] Decompression code
3953//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3954// Compressed with stb_compress() then converted to a C array and encoded as base85.
3955// Use the program in misc/fonts/binary_to_compressed_c.cpp to create the array from a TTF file.
3956// The purpose of encoding as base85 instead of "0x00,0x01,..." style is only save on _source code_ size.
3957// Decompression from stb.h (public domain) by Sean Barrett https://github.com/nothings/stb/blob/master/stb.h
3958//-----------------------------------------------------------------------------
3959
3960static unsigned int stb_decompress_length(const unsigned char *input)
3961{
3962 return (input[8] << 24) + (input[9] << 16) + (input[10] << 8) + input[11];
3963}
3964
3965static unsigned char *stb__barrier_out_e, *stb__barrier_out_b;
3966static const unsigned char *stb__barrier_in_b;
3967static unsigned char *stb__dout;
3968static void stb__match(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
3969{
3970 // INVERSE of memmove... write each byte before copying the next...
3971 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
3972 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
3973 if (data < stb__barrier_out_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
3974 while (length--) *stb__dout++ = *data++;
3975}
3976
3977static void stb__lit(const unsigned char *data, unsigned int length)
3978{
3979 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout + length <= stb__barrier_out_e);
3980 if (stb__dout + length > stb__barrier_out_e) { stb__dout += length; return; }
3981 if (data < stb__barrier_in_b) { stb__dout = stb__barrier_out_e+1; return; }
3982 memcpy(stb__dout, data, length);
3983 stb__dout += length;
3984}
3985
3986#define stb__in2(x) ((i[x] << 8) + i[(x)+1])
3987#define stb__in3(x) ((i[x] << 16) + stb__in2((x)+1))
3988#define stb__in4(x) ((i[x] << 24) + stb__in3((x)+1))
3989
3990static const unsigned char *stb_decompress_token(const unsigned char *i)
3991{
3992 if (*i >= 0x20) { // use fewer if's for cases that expand small
3993 if (*i >= 0x80) stb__match(stb__dout-i[1]-1, i[0] - 0x80 + 1), i += 2;
3994 else if (*i >= 0x40) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in2(0) - 0x4000 + 1), i[2]+1), i += 3;
3995 else /* *i >= 0x20 */ stb__lit(i+1, i[0] - 0x20 + 1), i += 1 + (i[0] - 0x20 + 1);
3996 } else { // more ifs for cases that expand large, since overhead is amortized
3997 if (*i >= 0x18) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x180000 + 1), i[3]+1), i += 4;
3998 else if (*i >= 0x10) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(0) - 0x100000 + 1), stb__in2(3)+1), i += 5;
3999 else if (*i >= 0x08) stb__lit(i+2, stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1), i += 2 + (stb__in2(0) - 0x0800 + 1);
4000 else if (*i == 0x07) stb__lit(i+3, stb__in2(1) + 1), i += 3 + (stb__in2(1) + 1);
4001 else if (*i == 0x06) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), i[4]+1), i += 5;
4002 else if (*i == 0x04) stb__match(stb__dout-(stb__in3(1)+1), stb__in2(4)+1), i += 6;
4003 }
4004 return i;
4005}
4006
4007static unsigned int stb_adler32(unsigned int adler32, unsigned char *buffer, unsigned int buflen)
4008{
4009 const unsigned long ADLER_MOD = 65521;
4010 unsigned long s1 = adler32 & 0xffff, s2 = adler32 >> 16;
4011 unsigned long blocklen = buflen % 5552;
4012
4013 unsigned long i;
4014 while (buflen) {
4015 for (i=0; i + 7 < blocklen; i += 8) {
4016 s1 += buffer[0], s2 += s1;
4017 s1 += buffer[1], s2 += s1;
4018 s1 += buffer[2], s2 += s1;
4019 s1 += buffer[3], s2 += s1;
4020 s1 += buffer[4], s2 += s1;
4021 s1 += buffer[5], s2 += s1;
4022 s1 += buffer[6], s2 += s1;
4023 s1 += buffer[7], s2 += s1;
4024
4025 buffer += 8;
4026 }
4027
4028 for (; i < blocklen; ++i)
4029 s1 += *buffer++, s2 += s1;
4030
4031 s1 %= ADLER_MOD, s2 %= ADLER_MOD;
4032 buflen -= blocklen;
4033 blocklen = 5552;
4034 }
4035 return (unsigned int)(s2 << 16) + (unsigned int)s1;
4036}
4037
4038static unsigned int stb_decompress(unsigned char *output, const unsigned char *i, unsigned int /*length*/)
4039{
4040 if (stb__in4(0) != 0x57bC0000) return 0;
4041 if (stb__in4(4) != 0) return 0; // error! stream is > 4GB
4042 const unsigned int olen = stb_decompress_length(i);
4043 stb__barrier_in_b = i;
4044 stb__barrier_out_e = output + olen;
4045 stb__barrier_out_b = output;
4046 i += 16;
4047
4048 stb__dout = output;
4049 for (;;) {
4050 const unsigned char *old_i = i;
4051 i = stb_decompress_token(i);
4052 if (i == old_i) {
4053 if (*i == 0x05 && i[1] == 0xfa) {
4054 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout == output + olen);
4055 if (stb__dout != output + olen) return 0;
4056 if (stb_adler32(1, output, olen) != (unsigned int) stb__in4(2))
4057 return 0;
4058 return olen;
4059 } else {
4060 IM_ASSERT(0); /* NOTREACHED */
4061 return 0;
4062 }
4063 }
4064 IM_ASSERT(stb__dout <= output + olen);
4065 if (stb__dout > output + olen)
4066 return 0;
4067 }
4068}
